# Welcome to OxaPay | OxaPay Docs

Welcome to the OxaPay Crypto Payment Gateway documentation. OxaPay provides a robust and secure platform for processing cryptocurrency payments, allowing businesses and developers to easily integrate cryptocurrency payments into their applications and websites.

### 

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/#what-is-oxapay)

What is OxaPay?

OxaPay is a leading crypto payment gateway that enables businesses to accept payments in various cryptocurrencies securely. With OxaPay, merchants can expand their customer base by offering a convenient and efficient payment method that leverages the benefits of blockchain technology.

### 

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/#what-is-the-oxapay-api)

What is the OxaPay API?

The OxaPay API is a powerful RESTful interface that allows developers to interact with their OxaPay accounts programmatically. It provides a comprehensive set of endpoints and methods to facilitate the creation and management of invoices, retrieval of real-time rate information, and processing of payments. The OxaPay API enables seamless integration of crypto payments into applications, e-commerce platforms, and websites.

### 

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/#who-is-this-documentation-for)

Who is this documentation for?

This documentation is designed for developers, merchants, and businesses who wish to integrate OxaPay's crypto payment gateway into their applications or websites. It provides comprehensive information about the OxaPay API, including endpoint descriptions, request and response examples, and use cases. Whether you are a developer looking to implement crypto payments or a merchant seeking to enhance your payment options, this documentation will guide you through the process of integrating and leveraging OxaPay's powerful crypto payment solutions.

Now that you have an overview of OxaPay and the purpose of this documentation, let's get started by creating an account and generating an API key.

[NextIntegrations](https://docs.oxapay.com/welcome-to-oxapay/integrations)

Last updated 2 months ago

---

# Payment Link | OxaPay Docs

Create crypto payment invoices effortlessly, without any coding knowledge and just a few clicks. Suitable for any type of business, these links are particularly advantageous for those without a website. Simply share the payment links with customers, get real-time updates on payment status, and receive payments efficiently. Streamline your transactions with reliability and ease. Customers can then make payments conveniently by clicking on the provided link. This integration simplifies the payment process and enhances the customer experience.

#### 

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/welcome-to-oxapay/integrations/payment-link#follow-these-steps-to-generate-payment-link)

Follow these steps to generate Payment Link:

1.  Log in to your OxaPay account.
    
2.  Navigate to the Payment Link page.
    
3.  Fill in the form, then click on the "Generate Payment Link" button.
    

#### 

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/welcome-to-oxapay/integrations/payment-link#watch-the-video-below-for-a-step-by-step-walkthrough-of-the-process)

Watch the video below for a step-by-step walkthrough of the process:

[![Logo](https://docs.oxapay.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fapp.oxapay.com%2Fmedia%2Flogos%2Ffavicon.ico&width=20&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=26d13ef6&sv=2)OxaPayapp.oxapay.com](https://app.oxapay.com/payment-link)

[PreviousIntegrations](https://docs.oxapay.com/welcome-to-oxapay/integrations)
[NextDonation Service](https://docs.oxapay.com/welcome-to-oxapay/integrations/donation-service)

# Payout Service | OxaPay Docs

OxaPay's Payout service allows businesses to automate and streamline cryptocurrency payouts, enabling efficient mass transfers to multiple recipients. This tool boosts operational efficiency, cuts costs, and ensures accurate payments, making it perfect for webmasters and businesses with frequent payouts. Ideal for rapid, secure fund distribution.

[![Logo](https://docs.oxapay.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fapp.oxapay.com%2Fmedia%2Flogos%2Ffavicon.ico&width=20&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=26d13ef6&sv=2)OxaPayapp.oxapay.com](https://app.oxapay.com/payout-service)

# Swap Service | OxaPay Docs

You can streamline your asset swaps using OxaPay's API. Our platform provides various tools and endpoints to help you identify swap pairs, assess swap rates, and calculate amounts. Begin by obtaining a General API key from your dashboard. With this key, access the swap request endpoint to execute swaps efficiently. This feature is designed to automate and enhance your trading processes, making it easier to manage digital assets directly through API integration.

[![Logo](https://docs.oxapay.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fapp.oxapay.com%2Fmedia%2Flogos%2Ffavicon.ico&width=20&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=26d13ef6&sv=2)OxaPayapp.oxapay.com](https://app.oxapay.com/swap)

# Merchant Service | OxaPay Docs

OxaPay Merchant Services streamlines the integration of cryptocurrency payments for businesses. Offering tools like crypto invoicing, white label solutions, and static addresses, these services cater to a variety of merchant needs. Begin by obtaining a Merchant API key, which enables secure, efficient crypto transactions.

# Donation Service | OxaPay Docs

Create a donation link to let visitors easily support your cause with cryptocurrencies like Bitcoin and Ethereum. With OxaPay, you can start receiving crypto donations in minutes, no technical skills required. Simply add a donation button to your website and share it on social networks like X and Instagram to expand your reach. OxaPay ensures a safe and swift process, making it easy for anyone around the world to support your cause.

#### 

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/welcome-to-oxapay/integrations/donation-service#follow-these-steps-to-generate-donation-link)

Follow these steps to generate Donation Link:

1.  Log in to your OxaPay account.
    
2.  Navigate to the Donation Link page.
    
3.  Fill in the form, then click on the "Generate Donation Link" button.
    

#### 

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/welcome-to-oxapay/integrations/donation-service#watch-the-video-below-for-a-step-by-step-walkthrough-of-the-process)

Watch the video below for a step-by-step walkthrough of the process:

# Plugins | OxaPay Docs

OxaPay offers dedicated digital currency payment gateway plugins for various popular eCommerce platforms, making it easier for merchants to integrate cryptocurrency payments into their online stores.

With these plugins, merchants can effortlessly add OxaPay's payment gateway functionality to their eCommerce platforms, allowing customers to choose cryptocurrencies as a payment option during the checkout process. The plugins are designed to ensure a smooth and secure payment experience for customers, while also providing merchants with real-time transaction updates and order management.

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/welcome-to-oxapay/integrations/plugins/wordpress/woocommerce)

![Cover](https://docs.oxapay.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F0cdQgWk1yvwE7MR49PSn%2Fblobs%2FQsNKsae6o1Zb054cs6q7%2Fwoocommerce.jpg&width=752&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=37036000&sv=2)

**WooCommerce**

WooCommerce is an open-source e-commerce plugin for WordPress. It is designed for small to large-sized online merchants using WordPress.

[Download Plugin](https://downloads.wordpress.org/plugin/oxapay.1.0.0.zip)

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/welcome-to-oxapay/integrations/plugins/wisecp)

![Cover](https://docs.oxapay.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2150865118-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F0cdQgWk1yvwE7MR49PSn%252Fuploads%252F3EGGZG6C5hf49v4Ygue0%252FGXNL_tNXUAASXW5%2520%281%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D54238ede-5c38-4d2f-a8cd-6d3cbd4999da&width=752&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9f6d1969&sv=2)

**WISECP**

WISECP is an all-in-one web hosting automation and management platform. It is designed for web hosting companies, domain registrars, and other online service providers

[Download Plugin](https://github.com/OxaPay/oxapay-wisecp/archive/refs/tags/v1.0.0.zip)

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/welcome-to-oxapay/integrations/plugins/clientexec)

# Clientexec | OxaPay Docs

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/welcome-to-oxapay/integrations/plugins/clientexec#what-is-clientexec)

What is Clientexec?


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Clientexec is a comprehensive billing and client management platform designed specifically for web hosting businesses. It allows companies to automate and streamline various aspects of their operations, including invoicing, customer management, and support.

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/welcome-to-oxapay/integrations/plugins/clientexec#key-features-of-clientexec)

Key Features of Clientexec:


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  **Automated Billing**: Manages invoicing, recurring payments, and integrates with multiple payment gateways, streamlining financial transactions.
    
2.  **Client Management**: Provides tools for customer support, including a ticketing system, and a customizable client portal where users can manage their accounts and services.
    
3.  **Service Management**: Automates the provisioning of services such as hosting accounts and domain registrations. It also supports customizable order forms for different products.
    
4.  **Customization and Extensibility**: Offers API access, plugin support, and custom fields to tailor the platform to specific business needs.
    
5.  **Security**: Features robust user permissions and SSL support to ensure data security and controlled access.
    
6.  **User Interface**: The platform is designed with a responsive, mobile-friendly interface for both admin and client areas, improving usability across devices.
    

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/welcome-to-oxapay/integrations/plugins/clientexec#oxapay-plugin-for-clientexec)

OxaPay Plugin For Clientexec


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Integrating OxaPay with Clientexec is a strategic move to expand your business and reach new milestones. The OxaPay plugin for Clientexec enables businesses to accept cryptocurrency as a full-fledged payment method, thereby broadening your customer base and enhancing payment convenience.

By using Clientexec, you can automate various aspects of your business operations efficiently. Enabling the OxaPay plugin on the Clientexec platform increases operational effectiveness and boosts customer engagement by facilitating crypto transactions with minimal fees and in the shortest time possible.

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/welcome-to-oxapay/integrations/plugins/clientexec#how-to-set-up-oxapay-plugin-for-clientexec)

How To Set Up OxaPay Plugin For Clientexec?


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  To install the OxaPay plugin ([Click here to download it](https://github.com/OxaPay/oxapay-clientexec/archive/refs/tags/v1.0.0.zip)
    ) for Clientexec, move the plugin folder to the following path _“Clientexec → plugins → gateways ”._
    
2.  The next step is to navigate to the web interface on Clientexec. Hover over the "Settings" tab in the top menu. Then, under the "Plugins" section, click on "Payment Processors."
    

![](https://docs.oxapay.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F0cdQgWk1yvwE7MR49PSn%2Fblobs%2Fqf76g7soU07xIWFwzBRd%2FScreenshot%2520%281167%29.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c01fb2e5&sv=2)

1.  Now that you are on the “Payment Processors” page, type "OxaPay" in the dropdown menu. When "OxaPay" appears, click on it to proceed to the plugin settings page.
    

![](https://docs.oxapay.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F0cdQgWk1yvwE7MR49PSn%2Fblobs%2FrBTuFqwpQPOE9O2nElwg%2FScreenshot%2520%281172%29.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=be52ae75&sv=2)

1.  Now, enter your "OxaPay merchant API key" in the designated field (you can find it in your OxaPay panel. If you don’t have an API key, [click here](https://docs.oxapay.com/welcome-to-oxapay/integrations/merchant-service)
     to learn how to create one, or you can use the "sandbox" mode for testing). Complete the remaining configurations, and then click on "Update Settings".
    

![](https://docs.oxapay.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F0cdQgWk1yvwE7MR49PSn%2Fblobs%2FkR2zZ11OSswtasNZK1b9%2FScreenshot%2520%281170%29.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2c580a8a&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/welcome-to-oxapay/integrations/plugins/clientexec#you-can-download-the-oxapay-plugin-for-clientexec-by-clicking-on-the-file-below)

# PrestaShop | OxaPay Docs

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/welcome-to-oxapay/integrations/plugins/prestashop#what-is-prestashop)

What is PrestaShop?


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

PrestaShop is an open-source e-commerce platform used to create and manage online stores. It allows users to build a fully customizable online shop with features for inventory management, payment processing, and shipping. PrestaShop is popular for small to medium-sized businesses due to its flexibility and a large marketplace of add-ons and themes.

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/welcome-to-oxapay/integrations/plugins/prestashop#key-features-of-prestashop)

Key Features of PrestaShop:


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  **Customizable Storefront**: PrestaShop provides an extensive selection of themes and templates, enabling merchants to fully personalize the appearance of their online stores. From color schemes to layout designs, everything is customizable to create a unique brand experience.
    
2.  **Product Management**: Managing your product catalog is made simple with robust tools that allow easy addition and organization of products. You can create detailed product listings with attributes such as size, color, and material, manage variations.
    
3.  **Multi-Language Support**: PrestaShop is built to cater to global markets by offering support for multiple languages and currencies. This enables businesses to sell to international customers, improving accessibility and boosting sales.
    
4.  **Payment Gateway Integration**: The platform integrates with a wide range of popular payment gateways, including OxaPay, PayPal, Stripe, and many others. This flexibility allows customers to choose their preferred payment method, improving conversion rates.
    
5.  **Advanced Reporting & Analytics**: The platform includes powerful reporting and analytics tools that provide in-depth insights into your store’s performance. You can access detailed sales reports, track customer behavior, monitor key performance indicators (KPIs), and analyze customer data to make informed business decisions.
    

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/welcome-to-oxapay/integrations/plugins/prestashop#oxapay-plugin-for-prestashop)

OxaPay Plugin For PrestaShop


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Integrating OxaPay with PrestaShop is a powerful step to grow your business and reach new heights. The OxaPay plugin for PrestaShop allows merchants to seamlessly accept cryptocurrency payments, opening up new possibilities for expanding your customer base and offering greater payment flexibility.

Enabling the OxaPay plugin on the PrestaShop platform improves operational efficiency and enhances customer experience by providing fast, low-fee crypto transactions as a fully integrated payment method.

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/welcome-to-oxapay/integrations/plugins/prestashop#how-to-set-up-oxapay-plugin-for-prestashop)

How To Set Up OxaPay Plugin For PrestaShop?


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  First, after logging into your PrestaShop admin panel, locate the "Modules" tab. Click on it, then select "Module Manager" from the dropdown menu.
    

![](https://docs.oxapay.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F0cdQgWk1yvwE7MR49PSn%2Fblobs%2F863BLCgGttqwteuj3Xon%2FScreenshot%2520%281280%29.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=154b9ea2&sv=2)

1.  Next, click on the "Upload a module" button and upload the OxaPay plugin file ([Click here to download it](https://github.com/OxaPay/oxapay-prestashop/archive/refs/tags/v1.0.0.zip)
    ).
    

![](https://docs.oxapay.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F0cdQgWk1yvwE7MR49PSn%2Fblobs%2FdwCBg4CkJy8lzYRPFn4W%2FScreenshot%2520%281279%29.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=54ce5aca&sv=2)

1.  The module installation will begin automatically. Once you see the message "Module installed" and the "Configure" button appears, click it to proceed.
    

![](https://docs.oxapay.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F0cdQgWk1yvwE7MR49PSn%2Fblobs%2FuwZElriZUtb12tCKiskq%2FScreenshot%2520%281281%29.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=72043357&sv=2)

1.  Enter your OxaPay Merchant API key (You can find this key in your OxaPay dashboard. If you don't have an API key, [click here](https://docs.oxapay.com/welcome-to-oxapay/integrations/merchant-service)
     for instructions on how to create one). Complete any other field. You can use the "sandbox" mode for testing. Once all the details are filled in, click "Save" to finalize the setup.
    

![](https://docs.oxapay.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F0cdQgWk1yvwE7MR49PSn%2Fblobs%2FsOLlKcCf7qwalJkHqnjf%2FScreenshot%2520%281284%29.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8f99b97d&sv=2)

# WISECP | OxaPay Docs

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/welcome-to-oxapay/integrations/plugins/wisecp#what-is-wisecp)

What is WISECP?


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

WISECP is next generation hosting and digital solutions automation. It includes a client area, admin area and a website interface. It has been developed for companies operating in the field of information technologies. With WISECP, all invoicing transactions, accounting (cash, income, expense) records, client management, product management, support services and many other operations can be carried out easily.

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/welcome-to-oxapay/integrations/plugins/wisecp#key-features-of-wisecp)

Key Features of WISECP:


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  **Client Management**: WISECP allows you to easily manage your client information, issue invoices, and view payment history.
    
2.  **Invoicing and Payments**: The platform enables automatic invoicing and payment management for clients, supporting various payment gateways.
    
3.  **Service Automation**: WISECP can automate the provisioning of web hosting, domain registration, and other services to clients. It handles the necessary configurations and sends access information to clients automatically.
    
4.  **Support and Ticketing**: WISECP includes a ticket management system that helps you respond to client requests and issues, ensuring more effective customer support.
    
5.  **Client Portal**: Your clients can manage their services, pay invoices, and communicate with your support team through a web-based client portal.
    
6.  **Reporting and Analytics**: WISECP provides various tools for generating reports on business performance, financial status, and client information, helping you make better decisions to improve your business.
    

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/welcome-to-oxapay/integrations/plugins/wisecp#oxapay-plugin-for-wisecp)

Using WISECP helps you automate your business operations in the most efficient way. By enabling the OxaPay plugin on the WISECP platform, you can increase effectiveness and customer engagement by facilitating all types of crypto transactions with minimal fees and in the shortest possible time.

    ) for WISECP, move the plugin folder to the following path _“WISECP → coremio → modules → payment”_.
    
2.  Go to the WISECP admin panel and follow the certain path _“setting → billing → payment gateways”._
    

![](https://docs.oxapay.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F0cdQgWk1yvwE7MR49PSn%2Fblobs%2Fz1NxzrK6FAt005zf7v8F%2FScreenshot%2520%281162%29.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8ae98dec&sv=2)

![](https://docs.oxapay.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F0cdQgWk1yvwE7MR49PSn%2Fblobs%2FqIQ8aGPyk93D68mq3HGp%2FScreenshot%2520%281201%29.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=655a6fea&sv=2)

![](https://docs.oxapay.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F0cdQgWk1yvwE7MR49PSn%2Fblobs%2FbErqzbJgt4M9OqTMWhSI%2FScreenshot%2520%281164%29.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=57ce17bc&sv=2)

1.  Now, enter your "OxaPay Merchant API Key" in the designated field (you can find it in your OxaPay panel. If you don’t have an API key, [click here](https://docs.oxapay.com/welcome-to-oxapay/integrations/merchant-service)
     to learn how to create one, or you can use the "sandbox" mode for testing). Complete the remaining configurations, and then click on "Save Settings".
    

![](https://docs.oxapay.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F0cdQgWk1yvwE7MR49PSn%2Fblobs%2FKE1nd1xj5VSjci7D76J1%2FScreenshot%2520%281165%29.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d7083819&sv=2)

# Blesta | OxaPay Docs

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/welcome-to-oxapay/integrations/plugins/blesta#what-is-blesta)

What is Blesta?


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Blesta is a comprehensive billing and client management platform designed primarily for web hosting companies and other service providers. It's a software solution that automates various aspects of a business, including billing, invoicing, client management, and support.

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/welcome-to-oxapay/integrations/plugins/blesta#key-features-of-blesta)

Key Features of Blesta:


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  **Billing Automation**: Automatically generates and sends invoices, handles both one-time and recurring payments, and supports various payment gateways.
    
2.  **Client Management**: Offers a centralized client portal for managing services, viewing invoices, and making payments, with support for multiple currencies and languages.
    
3.  **Service Provisioning**: Integrates with web hosting control panels and domain registrars to automate service management, supporting a wide range of digital services.
    
4.  **Support System**: Includes a built-in ticketing system, enabling businesses to provide customer support directly through Blesta.
    
5.  **Customizable and Extendable**: Features a modular design that allows for easy customization and the addition of new features through plugins and extensions.
    
6.  **Security**: Offers robust security measures like two-factor authentication (2FA) and data encryption, with regular updates to ensure security.
    
7.  **Reporting and Analytics**: Provides detailed reports on business metrics, with customizable dashboards for real-time monitoring.
    
8.  **Multi-Company Support**: Allows management of multiple companies or brands from a single installation, each with distinct settings and services.
    

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/welcome-to-oxapay/integrations/plugins/blesta#oxapay-plugin-for-blesta)

OxaPay Plugin For Blesta


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Integrating OxaPay with Blesta is a strategic step toward expanding your business and reaching new milestones. The OxaPay plugin for Blesta allows businesses to accept cryptocurrency as a fully integrated payment method, thereby widening your customer base and enhancing payment convenience.

By leveraging Blesta, you can efficiently automate various aspects of your business operations. Enabling the OxaPay plugin on the Blesta platform enhances operational efficiency and increases customer engagement by facilitating crypto transactions with minimal fees and rapid processing times.

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/welcome-to-oxapay/integrations/plugins/blesta#how-to-set-up-oxapay-plugin-for-blesta)

    ) for Blesta, move the plugin folder to the following path _“Blesta → components → gateways → nonmerchant”_.
    
2.  Navigate to the settings section within Blesta. Click on the "Payment Gateway" option in the settings page.
    

![](https://docs.oxapay.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F0cdQgWk1yvwE7MR49PSn%2Fblobs%2FbsUEuVERFt8P0QWtnPn5%2FScreenshot%2520%281175%29.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=55ece909&sv=2)

1.  In the "Available" section, locate the "OxaPay Payment Gateway" under the Non-Merchant category, and click on the "Install" button.
    

![](https://docs.oxapay.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F0cdQgWk1yvwE7MR49PSn%2Fblobs%2FMu6z9Hk8NBKIrw5coO2B%2FScreenshot%2520%281176%29-Recovered.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e836e42b&sv=2)

1.  Enter your OxaPay Merchant API key in the designated field. You can find this key in your OxaPay panel. If you don't have an API key, [click here](https://docs.oxapay.com/welcome-to-oxapay/integrations/merchant-service)
     to learn how to create one. Alternatively, you can use the "sandbox" mode for testing. After entering the Merchant API key, click on "Update Settings" to finalize the setup.
    

![](https://docs.oxapay.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F0cdQgWk1yvwE7MR49PSn%2Fblobs%2FGiYleXTZdmFZVhJcQ4gb%2FScreenshot%2520%281180%29.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e2dcd499&sv=2)

# Revoking Static Address | OxaPay Docs

You can revoke a static wallet by providing the merchant API key and the address associated with the static wallet. This action will disable the static wallet and prevent any further transactions from being credited to the specified address.

To avoid reaching the limit on generating new static addresses, we recommend manually revoking addresses with no transactions. If you have too many static addresses without transactions, the system will prevent you from generating additional ones. Therefore, it's important to proactively revoke inactive addresses to ensure you can continue generating new ones.

post

https://api.oxapay.com/v1/payment/static-address/revoke

Header parameters

merchant\_api\_keystringRequired

Your Merchant API Key for authentication and authorization.

Content-TypestringRequiredDefault: `application/json`

Body

application/json

application/json

addressstringRequired

The address of the static wallet you want to revoke.

Responses

200

Successful operation

application/json

Responseobject

Show properties

400

# OpenCart | OxaPay Docs

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/welcome-to-oxapay/integrations/plugins/opencart#what-is-opencart)

What is OpenCart?


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

OpenCart is a free, open-source e-commerce platform designed for building and managing online stores. It offers a user-friendly interface, a wide range of extensions, and supports multiple payment gateways, making it a popular choice for businesses looking to sell products online.

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/welcome-to-oxapay/integrations/plugins/opencart#key-features-of-opencart)

Key features of OpenCart:


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  **Store Management**: OpenCart offers a comprehensive admin panel that allows businesses to efficiently manage their products, categories, and customer accounts. With multi-store functionality, users can control multiple shops from a single interface, streamlining operations.
    
2.  **Payment Integration**: OpenCart supports various payment gateways such as OxaPay, PayPal, and others, making it easy for businesses to handle transactions. It also supports multiple currencies, ensuring smooth global payments and invoicing.
    
3.  **Product and Inventory Management**: The platform provides tools for managing a wide range of product options, attributes, and stock levels. This helps businesses organize their product catalog and track inventory efficiently.
    
4.  **Automation**: OpenCart offers automated features for order processing, shipping, and notifications. This helps reduce manual tasks, speeding up order fulfillment and enhancing the customer experience.
    
5.  **Analytics and Reports**: Built-in reporting tools provide valuable insights into sales, customer activity, and product performance. These analytics help businesses make data-driven decisions and track overall store performance.
    
6.  **Customer Management**: OpenCart includes customer account management, allowing store owners to track order history, handle communications, and manage customer reviews. Customers can also use a self-service portal to view orders and make changes to their accounts.
    

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/welcome-to-oxapay/integrations/plugins/opencart#oxapay-plugin-for-opencart)

OxaPay Plugin For OpenCart


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Integrating OxaPay with OpenCart is a great way to take your online store to the next level. The OxaPay extension for OpenCart enables businesses to accept cryptocurrency as a native payment method, providing customers with more payment options and expanding your market reach.

With the OxaPay integration, businesses can process transactions quickly and efficiently, with lower fees and faster settlement times compared to traditional fiat currencies. This makes it an attractive option for customers who prefer using cryptocurrencies for their purchases. Additionally, OxaPay offers robust security measures, ensuring that each transaction is secure and reliable, giving both merchants and customers peace of mind.

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/welcome-to-oxapay/integrations/plugins/opencart#how-to-set-up-oxapay-plugin-for-opencart)

How To Set Up OxaPay Plugin For OpenCart?


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Ensure that you have OpenCart version 4.x installed on your website. Once logged into your dashboard, go to the left menu, find the "Extensions" tab, click on it, and select "Installer".
    
2.  After that, upload the Oxapay plugin ([Click here to download it](https://github.com/OxaPay/oxapay-opencart/releases/download/v1.0.0/oxapay.ocmod.zip)
    ). Once you receive a successful upload message, go to the Oxapay bar in the action section and click on the "Install" button to complete the installation.
    

![](https://docs.oxapay.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2150865118-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F0cdQgWk1yvwE7MR49PSn%252Fuploads%252Fe129nm2uJIVnE1mKBy8S%252F1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc0159652-5e06-4a33-bc87-e3a5c02ec883&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a9eea8b6&sv=2)

1.  Now, first choose the "Payments" type from the list. Then, find the Oxapay bar and click on the "Install" button. After the installation is complete, click on the "Edit" button to configure the settings.
    

![](https://docs.oxapay.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2150865118-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F0cdQgWk1yvwE7MR49PSn%252Fuploads%252FZf1dh1xRZgBtzB6IQ3Gc%252F2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0db74240-aa12-4d94-aef7-cb3673b79728&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1bdab2c4&sv=2)

1.  Now, enter your "OxaPay Merchant API Key" in the designated field (you can find it in your OxaPay panel. If you don’t have an API key, [click here](https://docs.oxapay.com/welcome-to-oxapay/integrations/merchant-service)
     to learn how to create one, or you can use the "sandbox" mode for testing). Complete the remaining configurations, and then click on the "Save" button.
    

![](https://docs.oxapay.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2150865118-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F0cdQgWk1yvwE7MR49PSn%252Fuploads%252FVyBeeV2PVqY6gYTOKnCu%252F3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6a270c66-fa90-4ebb-8545-b570e59bba9b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d2257d10&sv=2)

# VirtueMart | OxaPay Docs

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/welcome-to-oxapay/integrations/plugins/virtuemart#what-is-virtuemart)

What is VirtueMart?


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**VirtueMart** is an **open-source eCommerce solution** designed to work with the **Joomla** content management system (CMS). It enables users to build and manage online stores with features that support product listings, customer management, orders, and payment processing.

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/welcome-to-oxapay/integrations/plugins/virtuemart#key-features-of-virtuemart)

Key Features of VirtueMart:


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  **Flexible Product Management:** VirtueMart enables easy management of products, categories, attributes, and variants, allowing administrators to efficiently organize and showcase their merchandise.
    
2.  **Multi-Language Support:** With built-in multi-language support, VirtueMart caters to international markets, allowing users to create and manage multilingual online stores.
    
3.  **Multiple Payment Gateways:** VirtueMart supports various payment gateways, including PayPal, Stripe, Authorize.Net, and more, offering flexibility in accepting payments securely.
    
4.  **Shipping and Tax Calculation:** The platform provides tools for calculating shipping costs and taxes based on different parameters such as weight, destination, and tax rates, streamlining the checkout process.
    
5.  **Inventory Management:** VirtueMart offers inventory management features, including stock tracking, low-stock notifications, and backorder management, helping users keep track of their inventory levels.
    
6.  **SEO-Friendly:** The platform is designed with search engine optimization (SEO) in mind, providing features such as customizable URLs, meta tags, and sitemaps to improve online visibility and rankings.
    
7.  **Extensions and Add-ons:** VirtueMart offers a wide range of extensions and add-ons, allowing users to extend the functionality of their online store with additional features and integrations.
    

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/welcome-to-oxapay/integrations/plugins/virtuemart#oxapay-plugin-for-virtuemart)

OxaPay Plugin For VirtueMart


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Integrating OxaPay with VirtueMart offers a modern and efficient way to accept cryptocurrency payments in your Joomla-based online store. This powerful combination enables businesses to easily accept crypto for products, providing a fast, secure, and borderless shopping experience for customers around the world.

With enterprise-level security, OxaPay ensures that all transactions are processed safely and reliably. This builds trust with your customers while expanding your store’s market reach. Enabling crypto payments in VirtueMart not only simplifies payment processing but also helps attract new customers and boost sales.

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/welcome-to-oxapay/integrations/plugins/virtuemart#how-to-set-up-oxapay-plugin-for-virtuemart)

How To Set Up OxaPay Plugin For VirtueMart?


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Go through the path “System -> Extensions” and upload the "OxaPay" plugin ZIP file ([Click here to download it](https://github.com/OxaPay/oxapay-virtuemart/archive/refs/tags/v1.0.0.zip)
    ) After that, the plugin must be activated in Plugins.
    

![](https://docs.oxapay.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2150865118-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F0cdQgWk1yvwE7MR49PSn%252Fuploads%252FtqtxJjS6pojq5TrpYri8%252FScreenshot%25202025-05-18%2520122527.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7f6b28e0-e80d-435d-a9ef-fb1b5c63ce1b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=656f1e29&sv=2)

1.  Go to Configuration and enter your OxaPay Merchant API key (You can find this key in your OxaPay dashboard. If you don't have an API key, [click here](https://docs.oxapay.com/welcome-to-oxapay/integrations/merchant-service)
     for instructions on how to create one). Complete any other fields. Once all the details are filled in, click "Save" to finalize the setup.

# Payout Status Table | OxaPay Docs

These are the possible payout statuses you may encounter while using the OxaPay Payout Service. Each status indicates the progress of the payout process, helping you track and manage payouts effectively.

Status

Description

processing

Request submitted and is being processed.

pending

Request has been processed and is now in the payment queue.

confirming

Transaction created and is awaiting confirmation on the blockchain.

confirmed

The transaction has been paid successfully.

canceled

Payout request was canceled.

rejected

The request was rejected for certain reasons.

[PreviousPayout History](https://docs.oxapay.com/api-reference/payout/payout-history)
[NextSwap](https://docs.oxapay.com/api-reference/swap)

Last updated 2 months ago

# Generate Static Address | OxaPay Docs

This endpoint allows you to generate a static address for a specific currency and network. The static address will be linked to a unique track\_id, and if a callback\_url is provided, your server will receive notifications for any payments made to the address. This enables you to track and receive transactions to the static address, regardless of the amount or timing.

> Please note that static addresses with no transactions for six months will be revoked.

post

https://api.oxapay.com/v1/payment/static-address

Header parameters

merchant\_api\_keystringRequired

Your Merchant API Key for authentication and authorization.

Content-TypestringRequiredDefault: `application/json`

Body

application/json

application/json

networkstringRequired

The blockchain network on which the static address should be created.

to\_currencystringOptional

The currency symbol of the cryptocurrency you want to convert to.

auto\_withdrawalnumber · decimal · max: 1Optional

1 indicates that the received currency will be sent to the address specified in your Address List on the Settings page and 0 indicates that the amount will be credited to your OxaPay balance.

callback\_urlstringOptional

The URL where payment information will be sent. Use this to receive notifications about payments made to the static address.

emailstring · emailOptional

Provide the payer's email address for reporting purposes.

order\_idstringOptional

Specify a unique order ID for reference in your system.

descriptionstringOptional

Provide order details or any additional information that will be shown in different reports.

Responses

200

Successful operation

application/json

Responseobject

Show properties

400

Bad request

application/json

post

/payment/static-address

Python

PythoncURLPHPNode.js

Copy

    import requests
    import json
    
    url = 'https://api.oxapay.com/v1/payment/static-address'
    
    headers = {
        'merchant_api_key': 'YOUR_MERCHANT_API_KEY',
        'Content-Type': 'application/json'
    }
    
    data = {
        "network": "TRON",
        "to_currency": "USDT",
        "auto_withdrawal": False,
        "callback_url": "https://example.com/callback",
        "email": "[email protected]",
        "order_id": "ORD-12345",
        "description": "Order #12345"
    }
    
    response = requests.post(url, data=json.dumps(data), headers=headers)
    result = response.json()
    print(result)

Test it

200

Successful operation

Copy

    {
      "data": {
        "network": "TRON",
        "to_currency": "USDT",
        "auto_withdrawal": false,
        "callback_url": "https://example.com/callback",
        "email": "[email protected]",
        "order_id": "ORD-12345",
        "description": "Order #12345"

# WHMCS | OxaPay Docs

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/welcome-to-oxapay/integrations/plugins/whmcs#what-is-whmcs)

What is WHMCS?


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

WHMCS (Web Host Manager Complete Solution) is a comprehensive web hosting management and billing software designed for online businesses. It automates various aspects of web hosting operations, such as client management, billing, support, and domain registration.

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/welcome-to-oxapay/integrations/plugins/whmcs#key-features-of-whmcs)

Key Features of WHMCS :


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  **Support System**: WHMCS includes a built-in support ticket system, knowledge base, and support department routing. This helps in managing customer support requests efficiently and provides a streamlined way for clients to get help.
    
2.  **Billing Automation**: WHMCS automates invoicing, payment processing, and reminders. It supports multiple currencies and integrates with numerous payment gateways like PayPal, Stripe, and others, making it easier for web hosting companies to manage their billing.
    
3.  **Domain Management**: The platform allows users to register, transfer, and manage domain names directly through WHMCS. It integrates with a wide range of domain registrars, enabling automated provisioning and management of domain services.
    
4.  **Automation**: WHMCS automates many tasks related to provisioning hosting accounts and managing renewals. This reduces the workload on administrators and improves service delivery speed.
    
5.  **Reporting and Analytics**: The platform provides detailed reports and analytics to track business performance, including sales, revenue, and customer activity.
    
6.  **Client Management**: It offers a complete client management interface, allowing businesses to manage client accounts, track order history, and handle communications efficiently. Clients can also log into a self-service portal to manage their services, pay invoices, and contact support.
    

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/welcome-to-oxapay/integrations/plugins/whmcs#oxapay-plugin-for-whmcs)

OxaPay Plugin For WHMCS


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Integrating OxaPay with WHMCS is a smart move to elevate your business to new heights. The OxaPay plugin for WHMCS allows businesses to accept cryptocurrency as a fully integrated payment option, expanding your customer base and offering greater payment flexibility.

The OxaPay plugin ensures that businesses can process payments quickly, with minimal transaction fees, and without the traditional delays associated with fiat currencies. This helps attract a broader audience, including customers who prefer using cryptocurrencies for their online purchases. Additionally, OxaPay's strong security features provide peace of mind, ensuring that every transaction is safe and reliable.

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/welcome-to-oxapay/integrations/plugins/whmcs#how-to-set-up-oxapay-plugin-for-whmcs)

How To Set Up OxaPay Plugin For WHMCS?


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  First, unzip the downloaded OxaPay plugin archive ([Click here to download it](https://github.com/OxaPay/oxapay-whmcs/releases/download/v1.0.0/oxapay_whmcs.zip)
    ) to your computer or directly on your hosting server.
    
2.  Locate the "oxapaygateway" folder and the "oxapaygateway.php" file from the unzipped archive. Move these to the following directory on your WHMCS installation: "_WHMCS → modules → gateways"._
    
3.  Transfer the Callback File: Next, find the **oxapaygateway.php** file located in the "callback" folder. Transfer this file to the following path on your WHMCS installation: _"WHMCS → modules → gateways → callback"._
    
4.  Now, hover over the settings icon, then select "Apps And Integrations" from the menu.
    

![](https://docs.oxapay.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F0cdQgWk1yvwE7MR49PSn%2Fblobs%2Fq3iPT838u9j0EXCwr79b%2FScreenshot%2520%281242%29.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=97433dc5&sv=2)

1.  Navigate to the "Search" tab and enter "OxaPay" in the search bar. In the results window that appears, click on "Activate" and proceed to the plugin settings.
    
2.  Now, enter your “OxaPay Merchant API Key” in the designated field. You can find this key in your OxaPay panel. If you don't have an API key, [click here](https://docs.oxapay.com/welcome-to-oxapay/integrations/merchant-service)
     to learn how to create one, or you can use the “sandbox” mode for testing purposes. After entering your API key, complete the remaining configuration settings and click on “Save Changes”.
    

![](https://docs.oxapay.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F0cdQgWk1yvwE7MR49PSn%2Fblobs%2FMAP8dLAsMPY5NSJVxHLC%2FScreenshot%2520%281246%29.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c68a2e3b&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/welcome-to-oxapay/integrations/plugins/whmcs#you-can-download-the-oxapay-plugin-for-whmcs-by-clicking-on-the-file-below)

You can download the OxaPay plugin for WHMCS by clicking on the file below:

44KB

[oxapay\_whmcs.zip](https://2150865118-files.gitbook.io/~/files/v0/b/gitbook-x-prod.appspot.com/o/spaces%2F0cdQgWk1yvwE7MR49PSn%2Fuploads%2FawBu44p7LqfuE5tumj2B%2Foxapay_whmcs.zip?alt=media&token=020604c5-4737-4ea6-b68d-7aef8e8a0a96)

# Static Address List | OxaPay Docs

Use this endpoint to retrieve a list of static addresses associated with a specific business. The list can be filtered by various criteria, such as trackId, address, network, email and orderId. Pagination is also available to fetch the results in smaller sets.

get

https://api.oxapay.com/v1/payment/static-address

Query parameters

track\_idintegerOptional

Filter addresses by a specific ID.

networkstringOptional

Filter addresses by the expected blockchain network for the specified crypto currency.

currencystringOptional

Filter addresses by the expected currency.

addressstringOptional

Filter static addresses by the expected address. It’s better to filter static addresses.

have\_txbooleanOptional

Filter the addresses that had transactions.

order\_idstringOptional

Filter addresses by a unique order ID for reference.

emailstring · emailOptional

Filter addresses by the email.

pageinteger · min: 1Optional

The page number of the results you want to retrieve.

Default: `1`

sizeinteger · min: 1 · max: 200Optional

Number of records to display per page.

Default: `1`

Header parameters

merchant\_api\_keystringRequired

Your Merchant API Key for authentication and authorization.

Content-TypestringRequiredDefault: `application/json`

Responses

200

Successful operation

application/json

Responseobject

Show properties

400

Bad request

application/json

get

/payment/static-address

Python

PythoncURLPHPNode.js

Copy

    import requests
    import json
    
    url = 'https://api.oxapay.com/v1/payment/static-address'
    
    headers = {
        'merchant_api_key': 'YOUR_MERCHANT_API_KEY',
        'Content-Type': 'application/json'
    }
    
    params = {
      'size': 20,
      'page': 1
    }
    
    response = requests.get(url, params=params , headers=headers)
    result = response.json()
    print(result)

Test it

200

      "data": {
        "list": [\
          {\
            "track_id": "133830568",\

# WooCommerce | OxaPay Docs

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/welcome-to-oxapay/integrations/plugins/wordpress/woocommerce#what-is-woocommerce)

What is WooCommerce?


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

WooCommerce is a free plugin for the WordPress content management system that allows users to easily set up and manage their online stores. It is one of the most popular and widely used tools for creating e-commerce websites. Due to its high flexibility and the ability to extend its functionality with various plugins and themes, WooCommerce is an ideal choice for both small and large businesses.

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/welcome-to-oxapay/integrations/plugins/wordpress/woocommerce#key-features-of-woocommerce)

Key Features of WooCommerce:


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  **Free to Use**: WooCommerce is available for free, allowing you to set up your online store without any additional costs.
    
2.  **Integration with WordPress**: WooCommerce is fully integrated with WordPress, enabling you to leverage all of WordPress’s capabilities.
    
3.  **Flexibility**: It offers high customization options through various themes and plugins, allowing you to design your store exactly how you want.
    
4.  **Product Management**: WooCommerce provides easy management of products, allowing you to add, delete, and edit products with details like pricing, images, descriptions, and categories.
    
5.  **Payment Gateways**: It supports multiple payment gateways, including local and international options, making it easy to receive payments from your customers.
    
6.  **Reporting and Analytics**: WooCommerce includes tools for reporting and analyzing your store's performance, helping you monitor and improve your business.
    
7.  **Multilingual Support**: With the help of various plugins, WooCommerce can be set up to support multiple languages, allowing you to serve customers from around the world.
    
8.  **Strong SEO Capabilities**: WooCommerce benefits from WordPress’s powerful SEO features, helping your store get better visibility in search engines.
    

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/welcome-to-oxapay/integrations/plugins/wordpress/woocommerce#oxapay-plugin-for-woocommerce)

OxaPay Plugin For WooCommerce


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Integrating OxaPay with WooCommerce is a strategic move to expand your business and achieve new milestones. The OxaPay plugin for WooCommerce enables businesses to accept cryptocurrency as a fully integrated payment method, thereby broadening your customer base and enhancing payment flexibility.

By leveraging WooCommerce, you can efficiently manage various aspects of your online store. Activating the OxaPay plugin on the WooCommerce platform boosts operational efficiency and enhances customer engagement by enabling crypto transactions with minimal fees and fast processing times.

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/welcome-to-oxapay/integrations/plugins/wordpress/woocommerce#how-to-set-up-oxapay-plugin-for-woocommerce)

How To Set Up OxaPay Plugin For WooCommerce?


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Log in to your WordPress control panel, navigate to the "Plugins" section, and click on "Add New". Select "Upload Plugin" then upload the "OxaPay" plugin ZIP file ([Click here to download it](https://downloads.wordpress.org/plugin/oxapay.1.0.0.zip)
    ) and click on the"Install Now" button.
    

![](https://docs.oxapay.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F0cdQgWk1yvwE7MR49PSn%2Fblobs%2FwMM2x0Wgkjes9zqzNfDF%2FScreenshot%2520%281183%29.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9eb8777a&sv=2)

1.  Once the plugin is installed, click on "Activate Plugin" to enable it.
    

![](https://docs.oxapay.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F0cdQgWk1yvwE7MR49PSn%2Fblobs%2FDcb0bx5LiQQTUUfPoH2T%2FScreenshot%2520%281185%29.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7dac00f4&sv=2)

1.  In the list of installed plugins, locate OxaPay and click on the "Configure" link.
    

![](https://docs.oxapay.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F0cdQgWk1yvwE7MR49PSn%2Fblobs%2FpK81LUpMfc61L8eEReYq%2FScreenshot%2520%281186%29.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=91fca684&sv=2)

1.  Enter your OxaPay Merchant API key (You can find this key in your OxaPay dashboard. If you don't have an API key, [click here](https://docs.oxapay.com/welcome-to-oxapay/integrations/merchant-service)
     for instructions on how to create one). Complete any other required fields. You can use the "sandbox" mode for testing. Once all the details are filled in, click "Save Changes" to finalize the setup.
    

![](https://docs.oxapay.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2F0cdQgWk1yvwE7MR49PSn%2Fblobs%2FTjd6VpgYB4LdHu0XCV9G%2FScreenshot%2520%281211%29.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5c6eba20&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/welcome-to-oxapay/integrations/plugins/wordpress/woocommerce#if-you-encounter-the-following-error)

If you encounter the following error:

> “There are no payment methods available. This may be an error on our side. Please contact us if you need any help placing your order.”

#### 

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/welcome-to-oxapay/integrations/plugins/wordpress/woocommerce#simply-navigate-to-the-checkout-page-in-the-pages-section-of-your-wordpress-admin-panel.-click-on-fo)

Simply navigate to the "Checkout" page in the "Pages" section of your WordPress admin panel. Click on "Form" and then select "Switch to classic checkout" to resolve the issue.

#### 

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/welcome-to-oxapay/integrations/plugins/wordpress/woocommerce#you-can-download-the-oxapay-plugin-for-woocommerce-by-clicking-on-the-file-below)

# Payout Information | OxaPay Docs

This endpoint retrieves the details of a specific payout using its track\_id. After generating a payout request, you will receive a track\_id, which can be used to obtain detailed information about the payout.

get

https://api.oxapay.com/v1/payout/{track\_id}

Path parameters

track\_idstringRequired

Unique identifier for the payout session.

Header parameters

payout\_api\_keystringRequired

Your Payout API Key for authentication and authorization.

Content-TypestringRequiredDefault: `application/json`

Responses

200

Successful operation

application/json

Responseobject

Show properties

400

Bad request

application/json

get

/payout/{track\_id}

Python

PythoncURLPHPNode.js

Copy

    import requests
    import json
    
    track_id = 'TRACK_ID'
    url = f'https://api.oxapay.com/v1/payout/{track_id}'
    
    headers = {
        'payout_api_key': 'YOUR_PAYOUT_API_KEY',
        'Content-Type': 'application/json'
    }
    
    response = requests.get(url, headers=headers)
    result = response.json()
    print(result)

Test it

200

Successful operation

Copy

    {
      "data": {
        "track_id": "258298351",
        "address": "1AmH3Qz2LooYa1YSyLhySuatwoRMsfznPJ",
        "currency": "BTC",
        "network": "Bitcoin Network",
        "amount": 0.02,
        "fee": 0.00001,
        "status": "processing",
        "tx_hash": "",
        "description": "test",
        "internal": false,
        "memo": "test",
        "date": 1736501470
      },
      "message": "Operation completed successfully!",
      "error": {},
      "status": 200,
      "version": "1.0.0"
    }

# Getting Started | Legacy | OxaPay Docs

To start using the OxaPay Crypto Payment Gateway, follow these steps:

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/legacy/getting-started#id-1.-create-an-account)

1\. Create an Account


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Visit the OxaPay website and sign up for an account. Fill in the required information and complete the registration process. Once your account is created, you will have access to the OxaPay dashboard.

Certainly! Here's the revised version of the "Generate an API Key" section, taking into account the two types of API keys available in OxaPay:

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/legacy/getting-started#id-2.-generate-api-keys)

2\. Generate API Keys


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

To interact with the OxaPay API, you need to generate two types of API keys: the Merchant API Key for processing payments and the Payout API Key for managing payouts. Follow these steps to generate your API keys:

### 

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/legacy/getting-started#merchant-api-key)

Merchant API Key

1.  Log in to your OxaPay account.
    
2.  Navigate to the Merchants API tab in your account.
    
3.  Click on the "Generate Merchant API Key" button.
    
4.  Give your Merchant API key a meaningful name for identification purposes.
    

Once generated, make sure to securely store your Merchant API key as it grants access to your OxaPay account for processing payments.

### 

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/legacy/getting-started#payout-api-key)

Payout API Key

In addition to generating a Payout API key for managing payouts, OxaPay provides an extra layer of security by allowing you to specify Allowed IPs for transfers. This feature restricts payout requests to be initiated only from the specified IP addresses, enhancing the security of your payout operations. Follow these steps to generate your Payout API key and configure the Allowed IPs for transfer:

1.  In your OxaPay account, go to the Payout API tab.
    
2.  Click on the "Generate Payout API Key" button.
    
3.  Provide a descriptive name for your Payout API key.
    
4.  Optionally, you can set the Allowed IPs for transfer in the provided field. Enter the IP addresses from which you want to permit payout requests.
    

Safely store your Payout API key as it provides access to the payout functionality of your OxaPay account.

By setting the Allowed IPs for transfer, you can ensure that payout requests can only be initiated from the specified IP addresses, adding an extra layer of security to your payout operations. This helps prevent unauthorized access and reduces the risk of fraudulent activity.

Remember to keep your Payout API key confidential and avoid sharing it with unauthorized individuals or third parties. This key grants access to the payout functionality of your OxaPay account and should be treated with the same level of security as your login credentials.

Once you have generated the Payout API key and configured the Allowed IPs for transfer, you can proceed with integrating the OxaPay Crypto Payment Gateway and utilizing the Payout API for managing payouts. Refer to the API Reference section for detailed information on using the Payout API key and performing payout-related operations.

If you have any questions or need further assistance regarding the configuration of the Allowed IPs for transfer or any other aspects of the Payout API, feel free to reach out to our support team.

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/legacy/getting-started#id-3.-test-the-api)

3\. Test the API


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Before integrating the OxaPay API into your application or website, it is recommended to test the API using the sandbox environment. The sandbox environment allows you to experiment and familiarize yourself with the API functionality without processing real transactions.

### 

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/legacy/getting-started#merchant-api-testing)

Merchant API Testing

To test the Merchant APIs and validate the available gateways, you can use the 'sandbox' as the merchant field in your API requests. This allows you to simulate payment flows and evaluate the response from the OxaPay system. Note that the sandbox environment is specifically available for testing purposes with the following format:

`merchant: 'sandbox'`

By including the 'sandbox' value as the merchant field in your Merchant API requests, you can access the test environment and perform various payment scenarios without impacting real transactions or balances.

During the testing phase, it is recommended to thoroughly explore the available API endpoints. These endpoints allow you to create payments, retrieve payment information, check transaction status, and more. By testing the API endpoints with different scenarios, you can verify the expected functionality and behavior of the OxaPay API.

Once you are confident with the testing results in the sandbox environment, you can proceed to integrate the OxaPay Crypto Payment Gateway into your live application or website. Make sure to update the merchant field to the appropriate value for production use.

Refer to the API Reference section for detailed information on available endpoints, request and response formats, and example code snippets to guide you through the integration process.

If you encounter any issues or have questions during the integration and testing process, our support team is available to assist you.

Let's dive into the API Reference section, where you will find detailed information about each API endpoint and how to use them effectively.

[PreviousIntroduction](https://docs.oxapay.com/legacy)
[NextIntegrations](https://docs.oxapay.com/legacy/integrations)

Last updated 2 months ago

# Generate Payout | OxaPay Docs

This endpoint enables you to generate a cryptocurrency payout request, allowing you to transfer funds to a specified address. It is designed to facilitate seamless and secure transactions by generating a payout request within your account.

post

https://api.oxapay.com/v1/payout

Header parameters

payout\_api\_keystringRequired

Your Payout API Key for authentication and authorization.

Content-TypestringRequiredDefault: `application/json`

Body

application/json

application/json

addressstringRequired

The recipient's cryptocurrency address where the payout will be sent.

currencystringRequired

The symbol of the cryptocurrency to be sent (e.g., BTC, ETH, LTC, etc.).

amountnumber · decimalRequired

The exact amount of cryptocurrency to be sent as the payout.

networkstringOptional

The blockchain network to be used for the payout. Required for currencies with multiple supported networks.

callback\_urlstring · uriOptional

The URL for sending payment status updates.

memostringOptional

A memo or tag for transactions on supported networks (e.g., for TON).

descriptionstringOptional

A description or additional information for the payout, useful for reports.

Responses

200

Successful operation

application/json

Responseobject

Show properties

400

Bad request

application/json

post

/payout

Python

PythoncURLPHPNode.js

Copy

    import requests
    import json
    
    url = 'https://api.oxapay.com/v1/payout'
    
    data = {
        "address": "RECEIVER_ADDRESS",
        "amount": 5,
        "currency": "TRX",
        "network": "TRC20",
        "callback_url": "https://example.com/callback",
        "memo": "Memo12345",
        "description": "Order #12345"
    }
    
    headers = {
        'payout_api_key': 'YOUR_PAYOUT_API_KEY',
        'Content-Type': 'application/json'
    }
    
    response = requests.post(url, data=json.dumps(data), headers=headers)
    result = response.json()
    print(result)

Test it

200

Successful operation

Copy

    {
      "data": {
        "track_id": "258298451",
        "status": "processing"
      },
      "message": "Operation completed successfully!",
      "error": {},
      "status": 200,
      "version": "1.0.0"
    }

# Introduction | Legacy | OxaPay Docs

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/legacy#welcome-to-oxapay)

Welcome to OxaPay


---------------------------------------------------------------------------

Welcome to the OxaPay Crypto Payment Gateway documentation. OxaPay provides a robust and secure platform for processing cryptocurrency payments, allowing businesses and developers to easily integrate crypto payments into their applications and websites.

### 

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/legacy#what-is-oxapay)

What is OxaPay?

OxaPay is a leading crypto payment gateway that enables businesses to accept payments in various cryptocurrencies securely. With OxaPay, merchants can expand their customer base by offering a convenient and efficient payment method that leverages the benefits of blockchain technology.

### 

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/legacy#what-is-the-oxapay-api)

What is the OxaPay API?

The OxaPay API is a powerful RESTful interface that allows developers to interact with their OxaPay accounts programmatically. It provides a comprehensive set of endpoints and methods to facilitate the creation and management of invoices, retrieval of real-time rate information, and processing of payments. The OxaPay API enables seamless integration of crypto payments into applications, e-commerce platforms, and websites.

### 

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/legacy#who-is-this-documentation-for)

Who is this documentation for?

This documentation is designed for developers, merchants, and businesses who wish to integrate OxaPay's crypto payment gateway into their applications or websites. It provides comprehensive information about the OxaPay API, including endpoint descriptions, request and response examples, and use cases. Whether you are a developer looking to implement crypto payments or a merchant seeking to enhance your payment options, this documentation will guide you through the process of integrating and leveraging OxaPay's powerful crypto payment solutions.

Now that you have an overview of OxaPay and the purpose of this documentation, let's get started by creating an account and generating an API key.

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/legacy#undefined)


------------------------------------------------

[API Reference](https://docs.oxapay.com/legacy/api-reference)

[NextGetting Started](https://docs.oxapay.com/legacy/getting-started)

# Generate White Label | OxaPay Docs

This endpoint allows you to generate white-labeled payment solutions, delivering a fully branded payment experience powered by the OxaPay gateway. Instead of generating an invoice URL, this endpoint provides comprehensive payment details, including the payment address, currency, amount, expiration time, and other relevant information, enabling you to manage the payment process within your own interface.

post

https://api.oxapay.com/v1/payment/white-label

Header parameters

merchant\_api\_keystringRequired

Your Merchant API Key for authentication and authorization.

Content-TypestringRequiredDefault: `application/json`

Body

application/json

application/json

pay\_currencystringRequired

Specify the currency symbol if you want the invoice to be paid in a specific currency. Defines the currency in which you wish to receive your settlements.

amountnumber · decimalRequired

The amount for the payment. If the currency field is not filled, the amount should be specified in dollars. If the `currency` field is filled, the amount should correspond to the specified currency.

currencystringOptional

Specify the currency symbol if you want the invoice amount calculated with a specific currency. You can also generate invoices in fiat currencies.

networkstringOptional

The blockchain network on which the payment should be created. If not specified, the default network will be used.

lifetimeinteger · min: 15 · max: 2880Optional

Set the expiration time for the payment link in minutes.

Default: `60`

fee\_paid\_by\_payernumber · decimal · max: 1Optional

Specify whether the payer will cover the invoice commission. 1 indicates that the payer will pay the fee, while 0 indicates that the merchant will pay the fee.

Default: `Merchant setting`Example: `1`

under\_paid\_coveragenumber · decimal · max: 60Optional

Specify the acceptable inaccuracy in payment. Determines the maximum acceptable difference between the requested and paid amount.

Default: `Merchant setting`Example: `10`

to\_currencystringOptional

The currency symbol of the cryptocurrency you want to convert to. You can only convert paid crypto currencies to USDT.

auto\_withdrawalbooleanOptional

1 indicates that the received currency will be sent to the address specified in your Address List on the Settings page and 0 indicates that the amount will be credited to your OxaPay balance.

callback\_urlstring · uriOptional

The URL where payment information will be sent. Use this to receive notifications about the payment status.

emailstring · emailOptional

Provide the payer's email address for reporting purposes.

order\_idstringOptional

Specify a unique order ID for reference in your system.

descriptionstringOptional

Provide order details or any additional information that will be shown in different reports.

Responses

200

Successful operation

application/json

Responseobject

Show properties

400

Bad request

application/json

post

/payment/white-label

Python

PythoncURLPHPNode.js

Copy

    import requests
    import json
    
    url = 'https://api.oxapay.com/v1/payment/white-label'
    
    headers = {
        'merchant_api_key': 'YOUR_MERCHANT_API_KEY',
        'Content-Type': 'application/json'
    }
    
    data = {
        "amount": 100,
        "currency": "USD",
        "pay_currency": "TRX",
        "network": "TRC20",
        "lifetime": 60,
        "fee_paid_by_payer": 1,
        "under_paid_coverage": 20,
        "to_currency": "USDT",
        "auto_withdrawal": False,
        "callback_url": "https://example.com/callback",
        "email": "[email protected]",
        "order_id": "ORD-12345",
        "description": "Order #12345"
    }
    
    response = requests.post(url, data=json.dumps(data), headers=headers)
    result = response.json()
    print(result)

Test it

Successful operation

# Error | OxaPay Docs

**API Error Responses**

When an error occurs in the OxaPay API, the response will be structured in a standardized format. This allows users to easily identify and address issues with their requests. Below is an overview of the error response structure, the possible status codes, and the types of errors you may encounter.

Error response structure

Copy

    {
      "data": {},
      "message": string, // A message containing additional information about the result of the request.
      "error": {
        "type": string,
        "key": string,
        "message": string
      } || {}, // An object that provides details about any errors that occurred.
      "status": integer, // The status of the request response. Typically provided as a numeric code (e.g., 200 for success or other codes for errors).
      "version": string // The version of the API being used.
    }

#### 

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/api-reference/error#statuses)

Statuses

**Status Code**

**Meaning**

**Common Causes**

**200 OK**

The request was successful.

The request was processed without errors.

**400 Bad Request**

The request was invalid or malformed.

Missing required fields, invalid data format, or unacceptable parameter values.

**401 Unauthorized**

The user is not authenticated or has invalid credentials.

Missing or invalid API key, incorrect session or token.

**404 Not Found**

The requested resource could not be found.

The resource doesn't exist or the endpoint is incorrect.

**500 Internal Server Error**

An unexpected server-side error occurred.

Server failure, issues with third-party integrations or dependencies.

**503 Service Unavailable**

One of the services is temporarily unavailable.

Server overload, service downtime, or maintenance.

[PreviousSystem Status](https://docs.oxapay.com/api-reference/common/system-status)
[NextWebhook](https://docs.oxapay.com/webhook)

# Payout History | OxaPay Docs

This endpoint retrieves a list of payout transactions associated with your account, based on your Payout API Key. You can filter the results by various criteria, including time range, status, amount, currency, network, type (internal or external), and more. Additionally, pagination allows you to retrieve the results in smaller, manageable sets.

get

https://api.oxapay.com/v1/payout

Query parameters

statusstringOptional

Filter payouts based on their status (processing, complete, rejected, etc.).

typestring · enumOptional

Filter payouts based on type.

Possible values: `external``internal`

currencystringOptional

Specify the currency symbol for filtering payouts in a specific currency.

networkstringOptional

Specify the blockchain network for filtering payouts on a particular network.

from\_amountnumber · decimalOptional

Specify the minimum payout amount for filtering.

to\_amountnumber · decimalOptional

Specify the maximum payout amount for filtering.

from\_dateintegerOptional

The start of the date window to query for payouts in UNIX format.

to\_dateintegerOptional

The end of the date window to query for payouts in UNIX format.

sort\_bystring · enumOptional

Sort the received list by a parameter.

Default: `create_date`Possible values: `create_date``pay_date``amount`

sort\_typestring · enumOptional

Display the list in ascending or descending order.

Default: `desc`Possible values: `asc``desc`

sizeinteger · min: 1 · max: 200Optional

Number of records to be displayed on one page.

Default: `10`

pageinteger · min: 1Optional

The page number of the results you want to retrieve.

Default: `1`

Header parameters

payout\_api\_keystringRequired

Your Payout API Key for authentication and authorization.

Content-TypestringRequiredDefault: `application/json`

Responses

200

Successful operation

application/json

Responseobject

Show properties

400

Bad request

application/json

get

/payout

Python

PythoncURLPHPNode.js

Copy

    import requests
    import json
    
    url = 'https://api.oxapay.com/v1/payout/'
    
    params = {
      'size': 20,
      'page': 1
    }
    
    headers = {
        'payout_api_key': 'YOUR_PAYOUT_API_KEY ',
        'Content-Type': 'application/json'
    }
    
    response = requests.get(url, params=params , headers=headers)
    result = response.json()
    print(result)

# Swap Rate | OxaPay Docs

This endpoint allows you to fetch real-time swap rates for cryptocurrency pairs supported by OxaPay. It’s ideal for applications that need the latest cryptocurrency prices to ensure accurate and timely calculations.

post

https://api.oxapay.com/v1/general/swap/rate

Header parameters

general\_api\_keystringRequired

Your General API Key for authentication and authorization.

Content-TypestringRequiredDefault: `application/json`

Body

application/json

application/json

from\_currencystringRequired

Specify the currency symbol you want to swap from.

Example: `BTC`

to\_currencystringRequired

Specify the currency symbol you want to swap to.

Example: `USDT`

Responses

200

Successful operation

application/json

Responseobject

Show properties

400

Bad request

application/json

post

/general/swap/rate

Python

PythoncURLPHPNode.js

Copy

    import requests
    import json
    
    url = 'https://api.oxapay.com/v1/general/swap/rate'
    
    data = {
        "from_currency": "USDT",
        "to_currency": "TRX"
    }
    
    headers = {
        'general_api_key': 'YOUR_GENERAL_API_KEY',
        'Content-Type': 'application/json'
    }
    
    response = requests.post(url, data=json.dumps(data), headers=headers)
    result = response.json()
    print(result)

# Swap Request | OxaPay Docs

This endpoint allows you to swap your account assets. You can swap one cryptocurrency for another instantly at the current market rate. To see the supported swap options, refer to the [swap pairs](https://docs.oxapay.com/api-reference/swap/swap-pairs2)
 endpoint. Whether you're swapping Bitcoin for Tether, Tether for Litecoin, or any other supported combination, this feature ensures secure and accurate asset swaps. Swaps are processed in real-time to provide you with the best available rates.

post

https://api.oxapay.com/v1/general/swap

Header parameters

general\_api\_keystringRequired

Your General API Key for authentication and authorization.

Content-TypestringRequiredDefault: `application/json`

Body

application/json

application/json

from\_currencystringRequired

Specify the currency symbol you want to swap from.

to\_currencystringRequired

Specify the currency symbol you want to swap to.

amountnumber · decimalRequired

Specify the amount of currency you want to swap.

Responses

200

Successful operation

application/json

Responseobject

Show properties

400

Bad request

application/json

post

/general/swap

Python

PythoncURLPHPNode.js

Copy

    import requests
    import json
    
    url = 'https://api.oxapay.com/v1/general/swap'
    
    data = {
        "amount": 0.5,
        "from_currency": "BTC",
        "to_currency": "USDT"
    }
    
    headers = {
        'general_api_key': 'YOUR_GENERAL_API_KEY',
        'Content-Type': 'application/json'
    }
    
    response = requests.post(url, data=json.dumps(data), headers=headers)
    result = response.json()
    print(result)

Test it

# Swap Pairs | OxaPay Docs

This endpoint allows you to access a list of swappable cryptocurrencies along with their minimum swap amounts. It provides the available options for the from\_currency and to\_currency fields when performing cryptocurrency swaps. Whether you're swapping Bitcoin for Tether or Tether for Litecoin, this list ensures clarity on supported pairs and their minimum swap requirements, helping you plan seamless transactions.

get

https://api.oxapay.com/v1/general/swap/pairs

Header parameters

general\_api\_keystringRequired

Your General API Key for authentication and authorization.

Content-TypestringRequiredDefault: `application/json`

Responses

200

Successful operation

application/json

Responseobject

Show properties
