# Payment Links | Legacy | OxaPay Docs

Payment links are a versatile tool offered by OxaPay that enables merchants to create customized payment URLs for their customers. With payment links, merchants can easily share payment requests through email, social media, or messaging platforms. Customers can then make payments conveniently by clicking on the provided link. This integration simplifies the payment process and enhances the customer experience.

### 

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/legacy/integrations/payment-links#create-your-account)

Create your account

You need an OxaPay account for managing and saving your crypto assets. You can create your OxaPay account free at this link (Just need an email and sign up in less than 1 minute):

[https://app.oxapay.com/signinapp.oxapay.com](https://app.oxapay.com/signin)

### 

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/legacy/integrations/payment-links#payment-link-page)

Payment link page

On the [Payment link](https://app.oxapay.com/paymentlink)
 page (you can find it in your OxaPay panel menu), you can view the details of your payment link.

![](https://docs.oxapay.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F517956072-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAQc1OXMAl6RP5j6dwH6R%252Fuploads%252FTWxQiZiWmbXKMGJF2txP%252FPicture1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd587520b-8f0c-4d52-8666-de731ce10e77&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=fd0abf7b&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/legacy/integrations/payment-links#generate-your-payment-link)

Generate your payment link

1\. Enter a desired name for your payment link, which should be between 3 and 30 characters long, in the "Name" field.

2\. Specify the payment amount in the "Price" field.

3\. Choose the accepted coins in the "Accepted Coins" section. Accepted coins refer to specific cryptocurrencies that are considered valid and can be used for payment. You can manually select specific coins or click on "Select All" to choose all coins.

4\. In the "Underpaid Cover" section, you can set a percentage between 0% and 60%. If the payer submits a payment that is slightly less than or equal to the underpaid amount, the invoice will still be accepted.

5\. If you enable the "Fee paid by payer", your customer will cover all the fees for this payment.

6\. Provide additional information or description about your payment link in the "Description" field.

7\. Finally, click on "Create Payment Link" to generate your desired payment link.

![](https://docs.oxapay.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F517956072-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAQc1OXMAl6RP5j6dwH6R%252Fuploads%252FlucEcgg7MbrYTtoYUg7P%252FPicture3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc7a5e681-7018-4c7e-816f-2aadcdb35a3a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3206ed03&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/legacy/integrations/payment-links#payment-summary)

Payment Summary

In this section, you can see the total value of payment transactions for today, this week, this month, and overall.

![](https://docs.oxapay.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F517956072-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAQc1OXMAl6RP5j6dwH6R%252Fuploads%252FlVdYC6nqFK6LHCRfjVfb%252FPicture2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc33a797d-d6bf-4f31-8361-c02422141b1c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1c6f4727&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/legacy/integrations/payment-links#payment-links-statistics)

Payment links statistics

In the "Payment links statistics " section, you can view a chart displaying the payment transactions associated with your payment link. This chart provides a visual representation of the payment activity, allowing you to track and monitor the performance of your payment link over time.

![](https://docs.oxapay.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F517956072-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAQc1OXMAl6RP5j6dwH6R%252Fuploads%252FlEPWWcqtAvS4V1dFHnVl%252FPicture4.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D39115667-0518-4bfc-83e8-cc81bffcf66f&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c8202cb&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/legacy/integrations/payment-links#your-payment-links)

Your payment links

In the "Your payment links" section, you can view the details of your payment link and you can copy the URL of your payment link or use its QR code. This allows you to easily share the payment link with others.

![](https://docs.oxapay.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F517956072-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAQc1OXMAl6RP5j6dwH6R%252Fuploads%252FrVxyeBXQKTs3jiEOrlCb%252FPicture5.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4b5abd74-642d-4ec4-9962-b4dcc0e04d0c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b4ba77a&sv=2)

Please note that the created payment links are not editable, and if any changes are required, you must delete that link and create a new one.

### 

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/legacy/integrations/payment-links#your-payment-links-transactions)

Your payment links transactions

In the "Your payment links transactions" section, you can view the details of your payment links transactions.

Please note that 'Amount' represents the invoice amount, 'Amount sent' is the amount paid, and 'Amount received' is the amount paid after deducting the transaction fee.

![](https://docs.oxapay.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F517956072-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAQc1OXMAl6RP5j6dwH6R%252Fuploads%252FCeEOjGrOdpivS0uT3Mbi%252FPicture6.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9f1849fb-e335-456a-bec2-6ecf1e679a57&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5ee56c6&sv=2)

# Merchant API | Legacy | OxaPay Docs

Merchants refer to webmasters or businesses who use OxaPay's services to integrate cryptocurrency payments into their websites. OxaPay's Merchants Webservice provides an API for webmasters to easily add crypto as a payment method on their websites, apps, and bots.

### 

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/legacy/integrations/merchant-api#create-your-account)

Create your account

You need an OxaPay account for managing and saving your crypto assets. You can create your OxaPay account free at this link (Need an email and sign up in less than 1 minute):

[https://app.oxapay.com/signinapp.oxapay.com](https://app.oxapay.com/signin)

### 

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/legacy/integrations/merchant-api#merchants-page)

Merchants page

On the [Merchants page](https://app.oxapay.com/merchant)
 (you can find it in your OxaPay panel menu), you can view the details of your Merchant keys.

![](https://docs.oxapay.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F517956072-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAQc1OXMAl6RP5j6dwH6R%252Fuploads%252FG933Q0vEgclVKefxqVym%252Fm-1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D52867c78-cc38-4c7a-8d78-e9a242e333fe&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=31fc7ba7&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/legacy/integrations/merchant-api#generate-your-merchant-api-key)

Generate your Merchant API key

1- Enter a desired name for your Merchant, which should be between 3 and 30 characters long, in the "Name" field.

2- Enter your logo’s URL in the “Logo URL” field. This logo will be displayed on your merchant payment page. The logo should have a transparent background and be in dark colors in PNG or SVG format.

3- Choose the accepted coins in the "Accepted Coins" section. Accepted coins refer to specific cryptocurrencies that are considered valid and can be used for payment. You can manually select specific coins or click on "Select All" to choose all coins.

4- In the "Underpaid Cover" section, you can set a percentage between 0% and 60%. If the payer submits a payment that is slightly less than or equal to the underpaid amount, the invoice will still be accepted.

5- If you enable the "Fee paid by payer", your customer will cover all the fees for this payment.

6- Finally, click on "Generate merchant API key" to generate your desired merchant key.

![](https://docs.oxapay.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F517956072-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAQc1OXMAl6RP5j6dwH6R%252Fuploads%252FsFNeRsI9ZuQbekOHi8OG%252Fm-3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D83af5bc8-38fe-498a-8304-198eb7ff2c62&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=864722b0&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/legacy/integrations/merchant-api#payment-summary)

Payment Summary

In this section, you can see the total value of the merchant’s transactions for today, this week, this month, and overall.

![](https://docs.oxapay.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F517956072-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAQc1OXMAl6RP5j6dwH6R%252Fuploads%252FlVdYC6nqFK6LHCRfjVfb%252FPicture2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc33a797d-d6bf-4f31-8361-c02422141b1c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1c6f4727&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/legacy/integrations/merchant-api#merchants-payment-statistics)

Merchants payment statistics

In the "Merchants payments statistics " section, you can view a chart displaying the payment transactions associated with your Merchant payment. This chart provides visual information about the Merchant key activity, allowing you to track and monitor the performance of your Merchant payments over time.

![](https://docs.oxapay.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F517956072-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAQc1OXMAl6RP5j6dwH6R%252Fuploads%252FL5PiuWZ1os5EfrbT25sD%252Fm-4.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dec5dfa61-73ba-4ac8-8973-4ed645f6748e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=aa4447ca&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/legacy/integrations/merchant-api#your-merchants-api-keys)

Your Merchants API keys

In the " Your merchant API keys " section, you can view the details of your merchant keys and you can copy the URL of your merchant key or use its QR code. This allows you to share the merchant key with others easily.

Please note that the created merchant keys are editable, and if any changes are required, you can click on the edit button in “Actions”.

![](https://docs.oxapay.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F517956072-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAQc1OXMAl6RP5j6dwH6R%252Fuploads%252Fcqtm5hnNvhdI2gHValwh%252Fm-5-highlight.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D020056b0-16fa-476d-9087-bd56129c1b62&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d6152d33&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/legacy/integrations/merchant-api#the-process-of-using-the-merchant-key)

The process of using the merchant key

After obtaining the merchant key, you can create an invoice, static address, and white-label Payment with the guidance provided in the [API references](https://docs.oxapay.com/api-reference)
.

### 

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/legacy/integrations/merchant-api#what-is-an-invoice-link)

What is an invoice link?

An invoice link is a dynamic payment link associated with a predefined expiration time and a specific invoice amount. Invoice links are typically generated for one-time use.

### 

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/legacy/integrations/merchant-api#how-to-create-an-invoice-link)

How to create an invoice link?

You can create your invoice link with the guidance provided in the [Creating an Invoice](https://docs.oxapay.com/api-reference/creating-an-invoice)
 in the API references.

### 

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/legacy/integrations/merchant-api#what-is-a-static-address)

What is a static address?

A static address is an address that remains valid indefinitely and has no restrictions on the amount or time of use.

### 

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/legacy/integrations/merchant-api#how-to-create-a-static-address)

How to create a static address?

You can create your static address with the guidance provided in the [Creating Static Wallet](https://docs.oxapay.com/api-reference/creating-static-wallet)
 in the API references.

### 

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/legacy/integrations/merchant-api#what-is-white-label-address)

What is white-label address?

A white-label address is a dynamic address associated with a predefined expiration time and a specific invoice amount. Unlike static addresses that remain constant, white-label addresses are typically generated for one-time use.

### 

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/legacy/integrations/merchant-api#how-to-create-white-label-payment)

How to create white-label Payment?

You can create your own white-label with the guidance provided in the Creating [White-Label](https://docs.oxapay.com/api-reference/creating-white-label-payment)
 Payment in the API references.

### 

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/legacy/integrations/merchant-api#your-merchant-transactions)

Your merchant transactions

In the "Your merchants transactions" section, You can view the details of your merchants' transactions.

Please note that the ‘Invoice amount’ refers to the entered defined amount of the invoice. 'Amount sent' is the amount paid, and 'Amount received' is the amount paid after deducting the transaction fee.

![](https://docs.oxapay.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F517956072-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAQc1OXMAl6RP5j6dwH6R%252Fuploads%252FIQ741jxW6XRAptXV8tbc%252Fm-6.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D709c0cc6-2f3b-475b-a6df-231c0283c235&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5916fa27&sv=2)

# Payout API | Legacy | OxaPay Docs

### 

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/legacy/integrations/payout-api#what-is-payout-api)

What is Payout API?

OxaPay's payout API is a feature that allows users to mass transfer crypto assets to other users automatically. This feature is particularly useful for webmasters.

#### 

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/legacy/integrations/payout-api#internal-payout-api)

Internal payout API:

This feature is especially beneficial for webmasters who need to make micropayments to their users. The internal Payout API offers the capability to transfer with zero fees and without any limits.

#### 

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/legacy/integrations/payout-api#external-payout-api)

External payout API:

This feature enables users to automate mass transfers of crypto assets to other users. However, please be aware that this option incurs fees and has limitations on the amount that can be transferred.

### 

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/legacy/integrations/payout-api#create-your-account)

Create your account

You need an OxaPay account for managing and saving your crypto assets. You can create your OxaPay account free at this link (Need an email and sign up in less than 1 minute):

[https://app.oxapay.com/signinapp.oxapay.com](https://app.oxapay.com/signin)

### 

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/legacy/integrations/payout-api#payout-api-page)

Payout API page

On the [Payout API page](https://app.oxapay.com/payout)
 (you can find it in your OxaPay panel menu), you can view the details of your Payout.

![](https://docs.oxapay.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F517956072-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAQc1OXMAl6RP5j6dwH6R%252Fuploads%252Fin1NL41FEmKQ1ntaRcEG%252Fpo1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D312d8cbb-b5dd-421c-86b5-c2d97fa513a8&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5bf77ec1&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/legacy/integrations/payout-api#generate-your-payout-api-key)

Generate your Payout API key

1-Right from the start, It is important to note that you need to enable 2FA (Two-Factor Authentication) for your account to use the payout API.

2-Enter a desired name for your Payout API, which should be between 3 and 30 characters long, in the "Name" field.

3-In the “Allowed IPs for transfer” field you can set some IPs and permit them to transfer. Any request for transfer from other IPs will fail.

4-The “Total daily transfer limit” field is for more security of your API transfers and if your total daily transfer exceeds this amount, the remained transactions will fail.

5-The “Transfer limit per transaction” field is for more security of your API transfers and transactions with more than this amount will fail.

6-In the “2FA verification code” field you should enter your 2FA code.

![](https://docs.oxapay.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F517956072-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAQc1OXMAl6RP5j6dwH6R%252Fuploads%252F4D4XzbtVI3XRaUTfEs3C%252Fpo4.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De3d62535-9883-438e-9567-bfc4338e5d10&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=78dfcae3&sv=2)

# Use Cases | Legacy | OxaPay Docs

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/legacy/use-cases#e-commerce-flow)

E-commerce Flow


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In an e-commerce scenario, merchants can leverage OxaPay's cryptocurrency payment gateway to offer customers the option to make purchases using various cryptocurrencies. The flow for this use case is as follows:

1\. The payer selects item/items for purchase, determining the total sum.

2\. The payer selects the preferred payment currency.

3\. The merchant generates a payment link using the OxaPay API's "Create an Invoice" endpoint. This endpoint allows the merchant to create a payment link with all the necessary payment details, such as the payment amount, currency, and other optional parameters like expiration time, feePaidByPayer, and underPaidCover.

4\. The API generates a unique payment link for the payer, containing the payment details.

5\. The payer receives the payment link and can click on it to proceed with the payment. Alternatively, the merchant can display the payment link on their website or send it via email or any other communication channel.

6\. When the payer clicks on the payment link, they are redirected to OxaPay's payment gateway to complete the payment.

7\. OxaPay's payment gateway displays the payment details and prompts the payer to select their desired cryptocurrency and network.

8\. After selecting the payment currency and network, OxaPay's payment gateway generates a specific payment address for the payer to send the cryptocurrency.

9\. The payer's crypto wallet application opens with the specified payment address pre-filled.

10\. The payer initiates the payment by sending the required cryptocurrency to the generated payment address.

11\. OxaPay's system monitors the transaction and updates the payment status in real-time.

12\. After a successful payment, the payer receives a payment confirmation alert on the page.

13\. The payer can then click on the "Return to Website" button to redirect to the merchant's specified returnUrl (if provided)

14\. The merchant's system receives a callback with payment information, such as transaction status, currency, amount, and fees.

15\. The merchant updates the order status and processes the purchase, allowing the payer to access their purchased goods or services.

16\. The merchant can access detailed payment-related information in their OxaPay accounts, providing transparency and easy management.

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/legacy/use-cases#e-commerce-with-seamless-payment-flow)

E-commerce with Seamless Payment Flow


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In an e-commerce scenario, merchants can leverage OxaPay's payment link feature to create a seamless payment experience for their customers. The flow for this use case, which includes the creation of a payment link, is as follows:

1\. The payer selects item/items for purchase, determining the total sum.

2\. The payer selects the preferred payment currency.

3\. The system retrieves the exchange rate for the selected currency and estimates the total amount in cryptocurrency.

4\. The merchant calls the "Create white-label" method to generate a payment link and obtain the payment address (e.g., a BTC wallet address for BTC payments).

5\. The payer is provided with the payment address and can initiate the payment by sending the required cryptocurrency to the given address.

6\. The payer can scan the QR code or manually copy the address and proceed with the payment using their preferred crypto wallet application.

7\. When the payer sends the cryptocurrency to the payment address, OxaPay's system receives a callback containing payment information, such as transaction status, currency, amount, and fees.

8\. The merchant's system updates the payment status based on the callback information, completing the purchase process.

9\. The merchant can access all payment-related information in their OxaPay accounts, ensuring transparency and easy management.

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/legacy/use-cases#investment-flow)

Investment Flow


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------

For investment platforms or websites, OxaPay offers a seamless crypto deposit and balance management flow. The steps for this use case are as follows:

1\. The user has a crypto balance on the website.

2\. The user selects the desired payment currency for making a deposit.

3\. The merchant calls the "Create static address" method to generate a permanent deposit address for the selected currency.

4\. The website displays the deposit address (e.g., BTC address) to the user, who can initiate the deposit by sending the cryptocurrency to the provided address.

5\. The user can scan the QR code or manually copy the address and proceed with the deposit using their crypto wallet application.

6\. After the user sends the cryptocurrency to the deposit address, OxaPay's system receives a callback containing deposit information, such as transaction status, currency, amount, and fees.

7\. The merchant updates the user's crypto balance based on the callback information, reflecting the deposited amount in the user's account.

8\. All relevant information about the deposit and user's balance is accessible in the merchant's OxaPay account.

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/legacy/use-cases#withdrawal-flow)

Withdrawal Flow


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In scenarios where users want to withdraw funds from their crypto balance on a website or platform, OxaPay simplifies the withdrawal process. The steps are as follows:

1\. The merchant has a crypto balance in their OxaPay account, which includes user funds.

2\. A user requests a withdrawal from their balance on the website.

3\. The merchant uses the OxaPay API's "/api/send" method to initiate a payout, providing the user's desired withdrawal address and amount.

4\. OxaPay's system sends the funds to the user's provided crypto address.

5\. After processing the payout, the merchant's system receives a callback containing transaction parameters, such as transaction status, currency, amount, and fees.

6\. The merchant updates the user's crypto balance, deducting the withdrawn amount from the user's account.

7\. The merchant can access comprehensive information about the transaction and balance in their OxaPay accounts, ensuring transparency and easy tracking.

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/legacy/use-cases#global-freelance-marketplace)

Global Freelance Marketplace


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1\. A global freelance marketplace connects freelancers and clients from around the world for various projects and services.

2\. To facilitate secure and efficient cross-border payments, the freelance marketplace integrates OxaPay's payment gateway.

3\. When a client hires a freelancer and agrees on a project's terms, they proceed to make a payment for the services rendered.

4\. The client selects their preferred cryptocurrency and network for payment on the freelance marketplace's payment page.

5\. OxaPay's payment gateway calculates the total amount in the selected cryptocurrency based on the current exchange rate.

6\. The client is redirected to OxaPay's payment gateway to complete the transaction.

7\. OxaPay's payment gateway generates a specific payment address for the client to send the cryptocurrency.

8\. The client's crypto wallet application opens with the payment address pre-filled.

9\. The client initiates the payment by sending the required cryptocurrency to the generated payment address.

10\. OxaPay's system monitors the transaction and updates the payment status in real-time.

11\. After a successful payment, the freelancer is notified of the payment and can proceed with the project.

12\. The freelancer delivers the completed project to the client through the freelance marketplace's platform.

13\. The client reviews and approves the project's completion.

14\. Upon approval, the freelance marketplace receives a callback from OxaPay's payment gateway with payment information, such as transaction status, currency, amount, and fees.

15\. The freelance marketplace releases the payment to the freelancer's account on the platform.

16\. The freelancer can access their earnings and withdraw funds to their crypto wallet at any time.

17\. The freelancer can view detailed payment-related information in their OxaPay accounts for transparency and financial tracking.

By integrating OxaPay's payment gateway, the freelance marketplace streamlines global payments for freelancers and clients, enabling them to transact in various cryptocurrencies securely and conveniently. The ability to select payment currency and network provides clients with flexibility in cross-border transactions, while real-time payment status updates ensure transparency and efficiency. Additionally, OxaPay's comprehensive payment information and management features enable the freelance marketplace to enhance financial tracking and provide a seamless payment experience for both clients and freelancers.

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/legacy/use-cases#online-gaming-platform-with-in-game-purchases)

Online Gaming Platform with In-Game Purchases:


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1\. Players on an online gaming platform want to make in-game purchases to enhance their gaming experience.

2\. The gaming platform integrates OxaPay's payment gateway to offer cryptocurrency payment options for in-game purchases.

3\. When a player decides to make an in-game purchase, the gaming platform prompts them to select their preferred cryptocurrency for payment.

4\. OxaPay's payment gateway calculates the total amount in the selected cryptocurrency based on the current exchange rate.

5\. The player is directed to OxaPay's payment gateway to complete the transaction. They can choose their desired cryptocurrency and network for payment.

6\. OxaPay's payment gateway generates a specific payment address for the player to send the cryptocurrency.

7\. The player's crypto wallet application opens with the payment address pre-filled.

8\. The player initiates the payment by sending the required cryptocurrency to the generated payment address.

9\. OxaPay's system monitors the transaction and updates the payment status in real-time.

10\. After a successful payment, the player receives a payment confirmation alert from their crypto wallet application.

11\. The player returns to the gaming platform, and the in-game purchase is instantly credited to their gaming account.

12\. The gaming platform receives a callback with payment information, such as transaction status, currency, amount, and fees.

13\. The gaming platform updates the player's account with the purchased in-game items or currency, providing them with an enhanced gaming experience.

14\. The gaming platform can access detailed payment-related information in their OxaPay accounts, ensuring transparency and seamless management of in-game purchases.

By integrating OxaPay's payment gateway, online gaming platforms can offer a secure, fast, and convenient way for players to make in-game purchases using various cryptocurrencies. The ability to select payment currency and network provides players with flexibility, while real-time payment status updates and payment confirmations ensure a smooth and reliable payment process. Additionally, OxaPay's comprehensive payment information and management features enable the gaming platform to streamline payment tracking and enhance the overall gaming experience for players.

These use cases demonstrate the versatility of OxaPay's cryptocurrency payment gateway, offering seamless payment processing, deposit management, and withdrawal functionalities to cater to various business needs. OxaPay's API integration provides the necessary tools and flexibility to enhance crypto-based transactions and offer an efficient payment solution for businesses and customers alike.

[NextTroubleshooting](https://docs.oxapay.com/legacy/troubleshooting)

# Blesta | Legacy | OxaPay Docs

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/legacy/integrations/plugins/blesta#what-is-blesta)

What is Blesta?


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Blesta is a comprehensive billing and client management platform designed primarily for web hosting companies and other service providers. It's a software solution that automates various aspects of a business, including billing, invoicing, client management, and support.

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/legacy/integrations/plugins/blesta#key-features-of-blesta)

Key Features of Blesta:


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  **Billing Automation**: Automatically generates and sends invoices, handles both one-time and recurring payments, and supports various payment gateways.
    
2.  **Client Management**: Offers a centralized client portal for managing services, viewing invoices, and making payments, with support for multiple currencies and languages.
    
3.  **Service Provisioning**: Integrates with web hosting control panels and domain registrars to automate service management, supporting a wide range of digital services.
    
4.  **Support System**: Includes a built-in ticketing system, enabling businesses to provide customer support directly through Blesta.
    
5.  **Customizable and Extendable**: Features a modular design that allows for easy customization and the addition of new features through plugins and extensions.
    
6.  **Security**: Offers robust security measures like two-factor authentication (2FA) and data encryption, with regular updates to ensure security.
    
7.  **Reporting and Analytics**: Provides detailed reports on business metrics, with customizable dashboards for real-time monitoring.
    
8.  **Multi-Company Support**: Allows management of multiple companies or brands from a single installation, each with distinct settings and services.
    

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/legacy/integrations/plugins/blesta#oxapay-plugin-for-blesta)

OxaPay Plugin For Blesta


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Integrating OxaPay with Blesta is a strategic step toward expanding your business and reaching new milestones. The OxaPay plugin for Blesta allows businesses to accept cryptocurrency as a fully integrated payment method, thereby widening your customer base and enhancing payment convenience.

By leveraging Blesta, you can efficiently automate various aspects of your business operations. Enabling the OxaPay plugin on the Blesta platform enhances operational efficiency and increases customer engagement by facilitating crypto transactions with minimal fees and rapid processing times.

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/legacy/integrations/plugins/blesta#how-to-set-up-oxapay-plugin-for-blesta)

How To Set Up OxaPay Plugin For Blesta?


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  To install the OxaPay plugin ([Click here to download it](https://github.com/OxaPay/oxapay-blesta/archive/refs/tags/v1.0.0.zip)
    ) for Blesta, move the plugin folder to the following path _“Blesta → components → gateways → nonmerchant”_.
    
2.  Navigate to the settings section within Blesta. Click on the "Payment Gateway" option in the settings page.
    

![](https://docs.oxapay.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F517956072-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAQc1OXMAl6RP5j6dwH6R%252Fuploads%252Fvy2EXtGbcNaB6Y2ht0iP%252FScreenshot%2520%281175%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfe33b049-8ad2-4ff3-8a77-0f7540afca63&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7cb2c9f0&sv=2)

1.  In the "Available" section, locate the "OxaPay Payment Gateway" under the Non-Merchant category, and click on the "Install" button.
    

![](https://docs.oxapay.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F517956072-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAQc1OXMAl6RP5j6dwH6R%252Fuploads%252FhADJteLeT38dRE3IXeeP%252FScreenshot%2520%281176%29-Recovered.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbd70d626-cdf9-401a-a776-8a263bebabb2&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=254a09e4&sv=2)

1.  Enter your OxaPay Merchant API key in the designated field. You can find this key in your OxaPay panel. If you don't have an API key, [click here](https://docs.oxapay.com/legacy/integrations/merchant-api)
     to learn how to create one. Alternatively, you can use the "sandbox" mode for testing. After entering the Merchant API key, click on "Update Settings" to finalize the setup.
    

![](https://docs.oxapay.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F517956072-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAQc1OXMAl6RP5j6dwH6R%252Fuploads%252FfqwBx0JsFSO9JHsEwZ7P%252FScreenshot%2520%281180%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D27ef11e5-17fb-4c35-a236-ce45fdae35df&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=32f3c990&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/legacy/integrations/plugins/blesta#you-can-download-the-oxapay-plugin-for-blesta-by-clicking-on-the-file-below)

You can download the OxaPay plugin for Blesta by clicking on the file below:

24KB

[oxapay\_blesta.zip](https://517956072-files.gitbook.io/~/files/v0/b/gitbook-x-prod.appspot.com/o/spaces%2FAQc1OXMAl6RP5j6dwH6R%2Fuploads%2FWqVR9zzNrVZ4ZBEEDFtD%2Foxapay_blesta.zip?alt=media&token=46a75b67-f9bf-40d6-82d4-657c3a59187a)

# WooCommerce | Legacy | OxaPay Docs

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/legacy/integrations/plugins/woocommerce#what-is-woocommerce)

What is WooCommerce?


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

WooCommerce is a free plugin for the WordPress content management system that allows users to easily set up and manage their online stores. It is one of the most popular and widely used tools for creating e-commerce websites. Due to its high flexibility and the ability to extend its functionality with various plugins and themes, WooCommerce is an ideal choice for both small and large businesses.

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/legacy/integrations/plugins/woocommerce#key-features-of-woocommerce)

Key Features of WooCommerce:


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  **Free to Use**: WooCommerce is available for free, allowing you to set up your online store without any additional costs.
    
2.  **Integration with WordPress**: WooCommerce is fully integrated with WordPress, enabling you to leverage all of WordPress’s capabilities.
    
3.  **Flexibility**: It offers high customization options through various themes and plugins, allowing you to design your store exactly how you want.
    
4.  **Product Management**: WooCommerce provides easy management of products, allowing you to add, delete, and edit products with details like pricing, images, descriptions, and categories.
    
5.  **Payment Gateways**: It supports multiple payment gateways, including local and international options, making it easy to receive payments from your customers.
    
6.  **Reporting and Analytics**: WooCommerce includes tools for reporting and analyzing your store's performance, helping you monitor and improve your business.
    
7.  **Multilingual Support**: With the help of various plugins, WooCommerce can be set up to support multiple languages, allowing you to serve customers from around the world.
    
8.  **Strong SEO Capabilities**: WooCommerce benefits from WordPress’s powerful SEO features, helping your store get better visibility in search engines.
    

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/legacy/integrations/plugins/woocommerce#oxapay-plugin-for-woocommerce)

OxaPay Plugin For WooCommerce


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Integrating OxaPay with WooCommerce is a strategic move to expand your business and achieve new milestones. The OxaPay plugin for WooCommerce enables businesses to accept cryptocurrency as a fully integrated payment method, thereby broadening your customer base and enhancing payment flexibility.

By leveraging WooCommerce, you can efficiently manage various aspects of your online store. Activating the OxaPay plugin on the WooCommerce platform boosts operational efficiency and enhances customer engagement by enabling crypto transactions with minimal fees and fast processing times.

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/legacy/integrations/plugins/woocommerce#how-to-set-up-oxapay-plugin-for-woocommerce)

How To Set Up OxaPay Plugin For WooCommerce?


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Log in to your WordPress control panel, navigate to the "Plugins" section, and click on "Add New". Select "Upload Plugin" then upload the "OxaPay" plugin ZIP file ([Click here to download it](https://downloads.wordpress.org/plugin/oxapay.1.0.0.zip)
    ) and click on the"Install Now" button.
    

![](https://docs.oxapay.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F517956072-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAQc1OXMAl6RP5j6dwH6R%252Fuploads%252FOWrsO2aPy12OZTEQKjxs%252FScreenshot%2520%281183%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D97557b0b-ad62-476c-b0ab-7c5e9b6b2303&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=982eeae7&sv=2)

1.  Once the plugin is installed, click on "Activate Plugin" to enable it.
    

![](https://docs.oxapay.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F517956072-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAQc1OXMAl6RP5j6dwH6R%252Fuploads%252F3ZheLQOpX6goFgMrfKwv%252FScreenshot%2520%281185%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dda37edfe-9f34-4ccb-803d-d940c366185e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=bf969351&sv=2)

1.  In the list of installed plugins, locate OxaPay and click on the "Configure" link.
    

![](https://docs.oxapay.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F517956072-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAQc1OXMAl6RP5j6dwH6R%252Fuploads%252FUlQhslXjvApsnYBf3Rin%252FScreenshot%2520%281186%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6c8b404a-9040-4e1e-b5e5-3eebb7261fbf&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7293c148&sv=2)

1.  Enter your OxaPay Merchant API key (You can find this key in your OxaPay dashboard. If you don't have an API key, [click here](https://docs.oxapay.com/legacy/integrations/merchant-api)
     for instructions on how to create one). Complete any other required fields. You can use the "sandbox" mode for testing. Once all the details are filled in, click "Save Changes" to finalize the setup.
    

![](https://docs.oxapay.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F517956072-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAQc1OXMAl6RP5j6dwH6R%252Fuploads%252FO9oZwT1CYduLrJDPawrn%252FScreenshot%2520%281211%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D561fa2c7-d71d-4a16-a134-cd08e1205166&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b949b960&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/legacy/integrations/plugins/woocommerce#if-you-encounter-the-following-error)

If you encounter the following error:

> “There are no payment methods available. This may be an error on our side. Please contact us if you need any help placing your order.”

#### 

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/legacy/integrations/plugins/woocommerce#simply-navigate-to-the-checkout-page-in-the-pages-section-of-your-wordpress-admin-panel.-click-on-fo)

Simply navigate to the "Checkout" page in the "Pages" section of your WordPress admin panel. Click on "Form" and then select "Switch to classic checkout" to resolve the issue.

#### 

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/legacy/integrations/plugins/woocommerce#you-can-download-the-oxapay-plugin-for-woocommerce-by-clicking-on-the-file-below)

You can download the OxaPay plugin for WooCommerce by clicking on the file below:

29KB

[oxapay.1.0.0.zip](https://517956072-files.gitbook.io/~/files/v0/b/gitbook-x-prod.appspot.com/o/spaces%2FAQc1OXMAl6RP5j6dwH6R%2Fuploads%2FdyYD4TFEKN6iujhsYzKa%2Foxapay.1.0.0.zip?alt=media&token=53f114bb-df8c-4562-a019-510fa6ed24e6)

# VirtueMart | Legacy | OxaPay Docs

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/legacy/integrations/plugins/virtuemart#what-is-virtuemart)

What is VirtueMart?


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**VirtueMart** is an **open-source eCommerce solution** designed to work with the **Joomla** content management system (CMS). It enables users to build and manage online stores with features that support product listings, customer management, orders, and payment processing.

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/legacy/integrations/plugins/virtuemart#key-features-of-virtuemart)

Key Features of VirtueMart:


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  **Flexible Product Management:** VirtueMart enables easy management of products, categories, attributes, and variants, allowing administrators to efficiently organize and showcase their merchandise.
    
2.  **Multi-Language Support:** With built-in multi-language support, VirtueMart caters to international markets, allowing users to create and manage multilingual online stores.
    
3.  **Multiple Payment Gateways:** VirtueMart supports various payment gateways, including PayPal, Stripe, Authorize.Net, and more, offering flexibility in accepting payments securely.
    
4.  **Shipping and Tax Calculation:** The platform provides tools for calculating shipping costs and taxes based on different parameters such as weight, destination, and tax rates, streamlining the checkout process.
    
5.  **Inventory Management:** VirtueMart offers inventory management features, including stock tracking, low-stock notifications, and backorder management, helping users keep track of their inventory levels.
    
6.  **SEO-Friendly:** The platform is designed with search engine optimization (SEO) in mind, providing features such as customizable URLs, meta tags, and sitemaps to improve online visibility and rankings.
    
7.  **Extensions and Add-ons:** VirtueMart offers a wide range of extensions and add-ons, allowing users to extend the functionality of their online store with additional features and integrations.
    

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/legacy/integrations/plugins/virtuemart#oxapay-plugin-for-virtuemart)

OxaPay Plugin For VirtueMart


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Integrating OxaPay with VirtueMart offers a modern and efficient way to accept cryptocurrency payments in your Joomla-based online store. This powerful combination enables businesses to easily accept crypto for products, providing a fast, secure, and borderless shopping experience for customers around the world.

With enterprise-level security, OxaPay ensures that all transactions are processed safely and reliably. This builds trust with your customers while expanding your store’s market reach. Enabling crypto payments in VirtueMart not only simplifies payment processing but also helps attract new customers and boost sales.

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/legacy/integrations/plugins/virtuemart#how-to-set-up-oxapay-plugin-for-virtuemart)

How To Set Up OxaPay Plugin For VirtueMart?


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Go to System -> Extensions, then upload the "OxaPay" plugin ZIP file ([Click here to download it](https://github.com/OxaPay/oxapay-virtuemart/archive/refs/tags/v1.0.0.zip)
    ) After that, the plugin must be activated in Plugins.
    

![](https://docs.oxapay.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F517956072-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAQc1OXMAl6RP5j6dwH6R%252Fuploads%252FmawOqmYOsGioRqY9oNTy%252FScreenshot%25202025-05-18%2520122527.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd79398e1-6efb-4331-8616-ef4e9c97c915&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f7e41336&sv=2)

![](https://docs.oxapay.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F517956072-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAQc1OXMAl6RP5j6dwH6R%252Fuploads%252FtiJk43Yaj8d5Ym0fy0it%252FScreenshot%25202025-05-18%2520123058.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df69a3537-a4f8-4311-a6dc-6d5d1f44da78&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d00e7cc4&sv=2)

1.  Now go to “Components -> VirtueMart -> Payment Methods” and then create a new payment method. Select the “VM Payment - OxaPay Crypto Payment Gateway” in Payment Method.
    

![](https://docs.oxapay.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F517956072-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAQc1OXMAl6RP5j6dwH6R%252Fuploads%252F1ssxtYPg7Wyg6OZMsMk3%252FScreenshot%25202025-05-18%2520124628.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1e98e4b8-a490-42ad-bf58-259aa49b8836&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7eca17c1&sv=2)

1.  Go to Configuration and enter your OxaPay Merchant API key (You can find this key in your OxaPay dashboard. If you don't have an API key, [click here](https://docs.oxapay.com/legacy/integrations/merchant-api)
     for instructions on how to create one). Complete any other fields. Once all the details are filled in, click "Save" to finalize the setup.
    

![](https://docs.oxapay.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F517956072-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAQc1OXMAl6RP5j6dwH6R%252Fuploads%252FkdsPUebEri2F31vPNz1A%252FScreenshot%25202025-05-18%2520124517.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D86684986-eaf4-42f3-af51-f3420f80e7c3&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8c2cdc83&sv=2)

**You can download the OxaPay plugin for VirtueMart by clicking on the file below:**

# OpenCart | Legacy | OxaPay Docs

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/legacy/integrations/plugins/opencart#what-is-opencart)

What is OpenCart?


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

OpenCart is a free, open-source e-commerce platform designed for building and managing online stores. It offers a user-friendly interface, a wide range of extensions, and supports multiple payment gateways, making it a popular choice for businesses looking to sell products online.

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/legacy/integrations/plugins/opencart#key-features-of-opencart)

Key features of OpenCart:


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  **Store Management**: OpenCart offers a comprehensive admin panel that allows businesses to efficiently manage their products, categories, and customer accounts. With multi-store functionality, users can control multiple shops from a single interface, streamlining operations.
    
2.  **Payment Integration**: OpenCart supports various payment gateways such as OxaPay, PayPal, and others, making it easy for businesses to handle transactions. It also supports multiple currencies, ensuring smooth global payments and invoicing.
    
3.  **Product and Inventory Management**: The platform provides tools for managing a wide range of product options, attributes, and stock levels. This helps businesses organize their product catalog and track inventory efficiently.
    
4.  **Automation**: OpenCart offers automated features for order processing, shipping, and notifications. This helps reduce manual tasks, speeding up order fulfillment and enhancing the customer experience.
    
5.  **Analytics and Reports**: Built-in reporting tools provide valuable insights into sales, customer activity, and product performance. These analytics help businesses make data-driven decisions and track overall store performance.
    
6.  **Customer Management**: OpenCart includes customer account management, allowing store owners to track order history, handle communications, and manage customer reviews. Customers can also use a self-service portal to view orders and make changes to their accounts.
    

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/legacy/integrations/plugins/opencart#oxapay-plugin-for-opencart)

OxaPay Plugin For OpenCart


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Integrating OxaPay with OpenCart is a great way to take your online store to the next level. The OxaPay extension for OpenCart enables businesses to accept cryptocurrency as a native payment method, providing customers with more payment options and expanding your market reach.

With the OxaPay integration, businesses can process transactions quickly and efficiently, with lower fees and faster settlement times compared to traditional fiat currencies. This makes it an attractive option for customers who prefer using cryptocurrencies for their purchases. Additionally, OxaPay offers robust security measures, ensuring that each transaction is secure and reliable, giving both merchants and customers peace of mind.

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/legacy/integrations/plugins/opencart#how-to-set-up-oxapay-plugin-for-opencart)

How To Set Up OxaPay Plugin For OpenCart?


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Ensure that you have OpenCart version 4.x installed on your website. Once logged into your dashboard, go to the left menu, find the "Extensions" tab, click on it, and select "Installer".
    
2.  After that, upload the Oxapay plugin ([Click here to download it](https://github.com/OxaPay/oxapay-opencart/releases/download/v1.0.0/oxapay.ocmod.zip)
    ). Once you receive a successful upload message, go to the Oxapay bar in the action section and click on the "Install" button to complete the installation.
    

![](https://docs.oxapay.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F517956072-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAQc1OXMAl6RP5j6dwH6R%252Fuploads%252FfdiFtceQDTN0lF212sxJ%252F1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0a86a793-408d-4774-8b2e-f31a9a7d958b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6dd0f1e1&sv=2)

1.  Now, first choose the "Payments" type from the list. Then, find the Oxapay bar and click on the "Install" button. After the installation is complete, click on the "Edit" button to configure the settings.
    

![](https://docs.oxapay.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F517956072-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAQc1OXMAl6RP5j6dwH6R%252Fuploads%252FPFggMzPqa1Wz0Pb6HJCj%252F2.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3c8562eb-42b7-44fe-970d-ca34f46585ca&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2205a851&sv=2)

1.  Now, enter your "OxaPay Merchant API Key" in the designated field (you can find it in your OxaPay panel. If you don’t have an API key, [click here](https://docs.oxapay.com/legacy/integrations/merchant-api)
     to learn how to create one, or you can use the "sandbox" mode for testing). Complete the remaining configurations, and then click on the "Save" button.
    

![](https://docs.oxapay.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F517956072-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAQc1OXMAl6RP5j6dwH6R%252Fuploads%252FUSULvIZe5aVjm4wOqYV4%252F3.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db7fc0fd7-084d-44ee-922d-0ca9fd9e2967&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=988e1d2a&sv=2)

**You can download the OxaPay plugin for OpenCart by clicking on the file below:**

15KB

# Easy Digital Downloads | Legacy | OxaPay Docs

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/legacy/integrations/plugins/easy-digital-downloads#what-is-easy-digital-downloads)

What is Easy Digital Downloads?


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Easy Digital Downloads (EDD) is a popular WordPress plugin designed for selling digital products like ebooks, software, and digital art. It provides an easy-to-use platform for managing downloads, payments, and customer data.

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/legacy/integrations/plugins/easy-digital-downloads#key-features-of-easy-digital-downloads)

Key Features of Easy Digital Downloads:


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  **Digital Product Management**: With the robust eCommerce platform that comes with a full-featured shopping cart, Easy Digital Downloads allows you to sell digital products with ease and manage your online store efficiently. With a user-friendly interface and a variety of customization options, Easy Digital Downloads is an excellent choice for anyone looking to sell digital goods online.
    
2.  **Get paid effortlessly**: Provides flexible payment options, including support for popular payment gateways like OxaPay, PayPal, Stripe, and Google Pay, as well as subscriptions, giving customers a range of options to pay in a way that suits them.
    
3.  **Intelligently designed:** The effects of site design on customer behavior are well-known. Easy Digital Downloads plays its role by including a base style that looks great as-is, but is also ready to integrate with any WordPress theme.
    
4.  **Unlimited file downloads:** Easy Digital Downloads is a platform for selling digital products that does not impose any additional bandwidth charges on file downloads. This means that you can sell and distribute your digital products without worrying about any extra fees based on the amount of data transferred to customers.
    
5.  **Automatic access control:** With Easy Digital Downloads, you can rest easy knowing that our secure file delivery system logs every customer interaction, giving you complete control over your business.
    

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/legacy/integrations/plugins/easy-digital-downloads#oxapay-plugin-for-easy-digital-downloads)

OxaPay Plugin For Easy Digital Downloads


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The OxaPay Plugin for Easy Digital Downloads (EDD) is a payment gateway integration that allows digital product sellers to accept payments through OxaPay, a cryptocurrency-based payment system. By integrating this plugin with EDD, store owners can offer their customers the option to pay using various cryptocurrencies, enhancing the flexibility of payment options and catering to a broader audience. The plugin seamlessly integrates into the EDD checkout process, ensuring a smooth and secure transaction experience without compromising usability or security.

In addition to offering cryptocurrency payments, the OxaPay plugin provides features like real-time exchange rate conversions, detailed transaction tracking, and automatic payment confirmations, reducing manual tasks for store owners. This plugin is particularly beneficial for businesses looking to expand globally, as it eliminates issues related to traditional currency conversion fees or regional payment restrictions, making it easier to cater to an international customer base.

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/legacy/integrations/plugins/easy-digital-downloads#how-to-set-up-oxapay-plugin-for-easy-digital-downloads)

How To Set Up OxaPay Plugin For Easy Digital Downloads?


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Log in to your WordPress control panel, navigate to the "Plugins" section, and click on "Add New". Select "Upload Plugin" then upload the "OxaPay" plugin ZIP file ([Click here to download it](https://downloads.wordpress.org/plugin/oxapay-payment-gateway-for-easy-digital-downloads.1.0.0.zip)
    ) and click on the"Install Now" button.
    

![](https://docs.oxapay.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F517956072-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAQc1OXMAl6RP5j6dwH6R%252Fuploads%252FaCedpYTVNSXMBoHEL3xb%252FScreenshot%2520%281313%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da3e2dc35-2a49-4f63-a19d-a8168ff1e85c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7af1ecab&sv=2)

1.  Once the plugin is installed, click on "Activate Plugin" to enable it.
    

![](https://docs.oxapay.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F517956072-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAQc1OXMAl6RP5j6dwH6R%252Fuploads%252FJiIGC6AZoqdzsoKxbxUw%252FPrestaShop-Logo.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5e401897-8528-46a4-8211-605439bc4339&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ac845dd9&sv=2)

1.  Go to your "Easy Digital Downloads" settings and navigate to the Payment section. After activating the OxaPay plugin, in the top bar, you will see an option for OxaPay. Click on it to configure the payment gateway settings.
    

![](https://docs.oxapay.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F517956072-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAQc1OXMAl6RP5j6dwH6R%252Fuploads%252F88VSW29NauXQigxVCitu%252FScreenshot%2520%281316%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D432d46dc-06eb-4fc0-b79c-607010657ecf&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3a7b6255&sv=2)

1.  Enter your OxaPay Merchant API key (You can find this key in your OxaPay dashboard. If you don't have an API key, click here for instructions on how to create one). Complete any other fields. You can use the "sandbox" mode for testing. Once all the details are filled in, click "Save Changes" to finalize the setup.
    

![](https://docs.oxapay.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F517956072-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAQc1OXMAl6RP5j6dwH6R%252Fuploads%252FP3m56g6s4iLudpRDzRWW%252FScreenshot%2520%281317%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0034bf4a-5705-4075-816c-644a46b2a428&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f7f2723c&sv=2)

# Paid Memberships Pro | Legacy | OxaPay Docs

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/legacy/integrations/plugins/paid-memberships-pro#what-is-paid-memberships-pro)

What is Paid Memberships Pro?


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Paid Memberships Pro is a popular WordPress plugin designed for managing and selling paid memberships. It allows site administrators to restrict access to content or services based on membership levels, offering exclusive content to paying members. With this plugin, you can set up multiple membership tiers, integrate various payment gateways, and manage access to premium content.

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/legacy/integrations/plugins/paid-memberships-pro#key-features-of-paid-memberships-pro)

Key Features of Paid Memberships Pro:


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  **Unlimited Membership Levels**: Create an unlimited number of membership tiers with varying prices and access privileges. Each level can offer unique benefits, allowing you to cater to different types of members or audiences.
    
2.  **Content Restriction**: Restrict access to specific content (such as posts, pages, categories, or custom post types) based on membership status. This lets you offer exclusive content to paying members while keeping general content available to all.
    
3.  **Flexible Payment Gateways**: Integrates seamlessly with popular payment gateways like OxaPay, PayPal, Stripe, and Authorize.net. You can offer different payment methods for your members and manage payments with ease, ensuring a smooth and secure transaction process.
    
4.  **Member Management**: Provides a detailed interface to manage your members, allowing you to view, edit, or update member profiles, change their membership level, or handle billing issues directly from the admin dashboard.
    
5.  **Reports & Analytics**: Track membership statistics with built-in reporting tools that give insights into revenue, active memberships, and overall growth. You can generate custom reports for better decision-making and optimization of your membership strategy.
    
6.  **Email Notifications**: Automate emails for critical events, such as membership signups, renewals, cancellations, and expiration reminders. Customize these email templates to communicate effectively with your members.
    
7.  **Add-ons & Integrations**: Expand the functionality of Paid Memberships Pro with a wide variety of add-ons, like affiliate tracking, WooCommerce integration, or custom member directories. This allows you to scale your membership site and add features as your needs grow.
    

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/legacy/integrations/plugins/paid-memberships-pro#oxapay-plugin-for-paid-memberships-pro)

OxaPay Plugin For Paid Memberships Pro


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The OxaPay Plugin for Paid Memberships Pr**o** is an extension designed to integrate the OxaPay payment gateway with the Paid Memberships Pro plugin, allowing websites to accept cryptocurrency payments for membership subscriptions. OxaPay is known for facilitating secure and efficient cryptocurrency transactions, offering users the ability to pay with various digital currencies like Bitcoin, Ethereum, and more. This integration expands payment options for membership-based websites, catering to customers who prefer using cryptocurrencies instead of traditional payment methods.

With this plugin, website owners can leverage the benefits of blockchain technology, such as faster transactions, lower fees, and broader international reach. The OxaPay plugin ensures a smooth checkout process, providing a seamless experience for members while maintaining compatibility with Paid Memberships Pro. This makes it a valuable solution for businesses seeking to diversify their payment options and attract a global audience.

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/legacy/integrations/plugins/paid-memberships-pro#how-to-set-up-oxapay-plugin-for-paid-memberships-pro)

How To Set Up OxaPay Plugin For Paid Memberships Pro?


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Log in to your WordPress control panel, navigate to the "Plugins" section, and click on "Add New". Select "Upload Plugin" then upload the "OxaPay" plugin ZIP file ([Click here to download it](https://oxapay.com/plugins/oxapay_pmpro.zip)
    ) and click on the"Install Now" button.
    

![](https://docs.oxapay.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F517956072-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAQc1OXMAl6RP5j6dwH6R%252Fuploads%252FPNRKXBSBGV6vqWZBRMHa%252FScreenshot%2520%289%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D788b60bd-280f-417a-88ba-2d39f3de3e22&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=40d694cd&sv=2)

1.  Go to your "Paid Memberships Pro" settings and navigate to the "Payment Gateway".
    

![](https://docs.oxapay.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F517956072-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAQc1OXMAl6RP5j6dwH6R%252Fuploads%252Fql1HvqoxTktKAztHL9l3%252FScreenshot%2520%2813%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D28a31ef0-257c-4f0e-a85c-1da039af76f2&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5144b3ce&sv=2)

1.  Enter your OxaPay Merchant API key (You can find this key in your OxaPay dashboard. If you don't have an API key, click here for instructions on how to create one). Complete any other fields. You can use the "sandbox" mode for testing. Once all the details are filled in, click "Save Settings" to finalize the setup.
    

![](https://docs.oxapay.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F517956072-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAQc1OXMAl6RP5j6dwH6R%252Fuploads%252FlOkeHxyr4FfH7Dio3oI6%252FScreenshot%2520%2812%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D397a38dd-6810-4a08-bb33-ea8d756347bf&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=86203788&sv=2)

# Gravity Forms | Legacy | OxaPay Docs

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/legacy/integrations/plugins/gravity-forms#what-is-gravity-forms)

What is Gravity Forms?


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Gravity Forms is a powerful WordPress plugin that allows users to create advanced and customizable forms with ease. It’s ideal for building contact forms, surveys, registrations, online payments, and more. Key features include a drag-and-drop interface, integration with third-party services (like OxaPay and PayPal ), and conditional logic to enhance user experience.

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/legacy/integrations/plugins/gravity-forms#key-features-of-gravity-forms)

Key Features of Gravity Forms:


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  **Ease of Use:** Gravity Forms provides a user-friendly drag-and-drop form builder, allowing you to create professional forms in minutes without requiring technical expertise.
    
2.  **Seamless WordPress Integration:** As a WordPress plugin, Gravity Forms integrates effortlessly with WordPress, enabling smooth performance and leveraging all of WordPress’s capabilities.
    
3.  **Customizable Forms:** With extensive field options and advanced settings, you can create contact forms, surveys, payment forms, registration forms, and more to suit your exact needs.
    
4.  **Payment Integrations:** Gravity Forms supports major payment gateways like OxaPay, PayPal, and Stripe, making it easy to accept payments, donations, or subscriptions directly through your forms.
    
5.  **Notifications and Confirmations :**Automate email notifications to inform both users and administrators upon form submissions, and customize confirmation messages or redirects to enhance user engagement.
    
6.  **Responsive Design:** Forms created with Gravity Forms are mobile-friendly and responsive, ensuring they function perfectly across all devices, including tablets and smartphones.
    

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/legacy/integrations/plugins/gravity-forms#oxapay-plugin-for-gravity-forms)

OxaPay Plugin For Gravity Forms


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Integrating OxaPay with Gravity Forms is a strategic way to enhance your payment options and reach a broader audience. The OxaPay integration enables businesses to seamlessly accept cryptocurrency payments directly through Gravity Forms, offering customers greater flexibility and modernizing your payment process.

Additionally, OxaPay prioritizes security, ensuring that every transaction is safe, reliable, and protected. By adding cryptocurrency as a payment option inGravity Forms, businesses can attract a wider customer base while streamlining their payment workflows and improving the overall user experience.

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/legacy/integrations/plugins/gravity-forms#how-to-set-up-oxapay-plugin-for-gravity-forms)

How To Set Up OxaPay Plugin For Gravity Forms?

    ) and click on the"Install Now" button.
    

![](https://docs.oxapay.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F517956072-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAQc1OXMAl6RP5j6dwH6R%252Fuploads%252FFSunSCN1Ru1ko1yp7SuL%252FScreenshot%2520%2858%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd9648e78-5664-4889-a917-78918985b744&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c2e18ef4&sv=2)

     for instructions on how to create one). Complete any other required fields. You can use the "sandbox" mode for testing. Once all the details are filled in, click "Save Settings" to finalize the setup.

# PrestaShop | Legacy | OxaPay Docs

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/legacy/integrations/plugins/prestashop#what-is-prestashop)

What is PrestaShop?


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

PrestaShop is an open-source e-commerce platform used to create and manage online stores. It allows users to build a fully customizable online shop with features for inventory management, payment processing, and shipping. PrestaShop is popular for small to medium-sized businesses due to its flexibility and a large marketplace of add-ons and themes.

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/legacy/integrations/plugins/prestashop#key-features-of-prestashop)

Key Features of PrestaShop:


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  **Customizable Storefront**: PrestaShop provides an extensive selection of themes and templates, enabling merchants to fully personalize the appearance of their online stores. From color schemes to layout designs, everything is customizable to create a unique brand experience.
    
2.  **Product Management**: Managing your product catalog is made simple with robust tools that allow easy addition and organization of products. You can create detailed product listings with attributes such as size, color, and material, manage variations.
    
3.  **Multi-Language Support**: PrestaShop is built to cater to global markets by offering support for multiple languages and currencies. This enables businesses to sell to international customers, improving accessibility and boosting sales.
    
4.  **Payment Gateway Integration**: The platform integrates with a wide range of popular payment gateways, including OxaPay, PayPal, Stripe, and many others. This flexibility allows customers to choose their preferred payment method, improving conversion rates.
    
5.  **Advanced Reporting & Analytics**: The platform includes powerful reporting and analytics tools that provide in-depth insights into your store’s performance. You can access detailed sales reports, track customer behavior, monitor key performance indicators (KPIs), and analyze customer data to make informed business decisions.
    

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/legacy/integrations/plugins/prestashop#oxapay-plugin-for-prestashop)

OxaPay Plugin For PrestaShop


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Integrating OxaPay with PrestaShop is a powerful step to grow your business and reach new heights. The OxaPay plugin for PrestaShop allows merchants to seamlessly accept cryptocurrency payments, opening up new possibilities for expanding your customer base and offering greater payment flexibility.

Enabling the OxaPay plugin on the PrestaShop platform improves operational efficiency and enhances customer experience by providing fast, low-fee crypto transactions as a fully integrated payment method.

[](https://docs.oxapay.com/legacy/integrations/plugins/prestashop#how-to-set-up-oxapay-plugin-for-prestashop)

How To Set Up OxaPay Plugin For PrestaShop?


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  First, after logging into your PrestaShop admin panel, locate the "Modules" tab. Click on it, then select "Module Manager" from the dropdown menu.
    

![](https://docs.oxapay.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F517956072-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAQc1OXMAl6RP5j6dwH6R%252Fuploads%252FjMA7V84doFz9dd6ByVr7%252FScreenshot%2520%281280%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Deb38f894-01a1-49b6-860c-9b8999c56dc5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=fd45ec44&sv=2)

1.  Next, click on the "Upload a module" button and upload the OxaPay plugin file ([Click here to download it](https://github.com/OxaPay/oxapay-prestashop/archive/refs/tags/v1.0.0.zip)
    ).
    

![](https://docs.oxapay.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F517956072-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAQc1OXMAl6RP5j6dwH6R%252Fuploads%252FDju2mwJ0UCY3VGH5hOxs%252FScreenshot%2520%281279%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D03c12cfa-bcde-4a8d-a357-917772b6012d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3da15ef6&sv=2)

1.  The module installation will begin automatically. Once you see the message "Module installed" and the "Configure" button appears, click it to proceed.
    

![](https://docs.oxapay.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F517956072-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAQc1OXMAl6RP5j6dwH6R%252Fuploads%252FVDnA48lMXNXaxD6mw3Op%252FScreenshot%2520%281281%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Def127ce8-dedb-41a4-a2a2-4ad16b8772f3&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=fec1112a&sv=2)

1.  Enter your OxaPay Merchant API key (You can find this key in your OxaPay dashboard. If you don't have an API key, [click here](https://docs.oxapay.com/legacy/integrations/merchant-api)
     for instructions on how to create one). Complete any other field. You can use the "sandbox" mode for testing. Once all the details are filled in, click "Save" to finalize the setup.
    

![](https://docs.oxapay.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F517956072-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FAQc1OXMAl6RP5j6dwH6R%252Fuploads%252Fn8SwWpc5osiO5H9iD67w%252FScreenshot%2520%281284%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8473fcae-d8bf-4b45-95e0-2535ca588b40&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4b6af18&sv=2)
